Letter from the Grain Industry to the Chamber of Commerce 128

Sharing by Shares vs. Joint Liability

Clear Advantages and Disadvantages, Please Chamber of Commerce Strive

The local Grain, Oil Cake Industry Association, Bean and Rice Industry Association, etc., yesterday, due to the Legislative Yuan's Commercial Law Committee sending Huang Youchang as a member to Shanghai to investigate the commercial registration law of the grain and bean rice industry, notified by the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to express opinions as much as possible, the associations specially sent a detailed letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce regarding the reasons for partnership business and sharing by shares. The original letter stated: "Respectfully, Previously, Article 681 of our country's current civil law, regarding joint liability for partnership debts, greatly conflicted with our country's inherent commercial customs. Our association, etc., based on legal principles and citing partnership regulations from the civil laws of Germany, France, Switzerland, and Japan, petitioned your esteemed association to forward it to the Legislative Yuan for modification. As a result, the remedy for partnership organizations, sharing by shares, can be remedied by separately establishing commercial registration. The Civil and Commercial Law Committee is drafting the regulations. Now, We received a notice from your esteemed association that the Commercial Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan stated in a letter that our committee is currently drafting a commercial registration law and needs to investigate the commercial situation in various places for reference. Huang Youchang has been dispatched to Shanghai for investigation. In addition to copying and sending the opinions of various industries regarding the case of sharing responsibility for partnerships for reference, what opinions do you have regarding the commercial registration law? Please express them as much as possible in a letter and forward them to our committee for review and submission. According to this, our association has already fully stated the reasons for sharing by shares in partnerships last year, referring to the legal reasons of various countries, with our association taking the lead, together with various industry associations, and refuted the opinions advocated by accountant Pan Xulun. The esteemed association forwarded it to the Legislative Yuan for submission to the Civil and Commercial Law Committees. After repeated discussions, a separate commercial registration law was finally established to carry out remedies. Now, the Legislative Yuan is about to draft the commercial registration law and has first sent Huang Youchang to Shanghai for investigation and to solicit opinions from our association, etc., showing that the Legislative Yuan respects public opinion and is considerate of commercial conditions, and that your esteemed association can extensively consult and follow the will and customs of various groups. In addition to requesting your esteemed association to still copy and send the reasons stated last year for reference, now the association will again open up opinions on the reasons for sharing by shares in partnership business in substantive law and procedural law, requesting your esteemed association to grant adoption and forward them on our behalf, for which we will be infinitely grateful: (1) Article 681 of the current civil law, regarding partnership contracts, should be changed to sharing by shares. In addition to already clearly stating the convenience based on the laws of various European and Asian countries last year, now our association believes that the partnership business in our country should be shared by shares, and there are still old laws in our country that can be cited as evidence. When the Law Compilation Institute of the former Qing Dynasty compiled the draft of the civil law, although the purpose of the legislation at that time and the general meaning of compiling the general rules of the civil law, real rights, and creditor's rights, the first three compilations, were quite different from the principles of the current civil and commercial laws combined, the partnership business still fell within the scope of the contract in the second chapter of the first compilation of the draft. Article 797 of the draft civil law of the former Qing Dynasty stated that if there is no special agreement among the partners, the joint investment must be equally divided. Also, Article 809 of the same draft stated that if the percentage of profit and loss distribution among the partners is not agreed upon, regardless of the type and amount of investment, it shall be equally divided. Also, Article 828 of the same draft stated that if the partnership property is not sufficient to repay the partnership debts and the investment of each partner, each partner must bear the insufficient amount according to the percentage of loss distribution. According to this, the draft civil law only stipulated equal division of all loss sharing for partnership business and did not explicitly state joint liability. The draft has never been formally implemented and promulgated, but the precedents and interpretations of the Supreme Court at that time, Although this draft has never been recognized as a formally effective law, it is not without some precedents for the adoption of the academic theory and the consideration of the regulations. All those who study law and those in the legal profession deeply understand this purpose. The reason for this provision at that time was to follow the inherent customs of our country and to slightly imitate the spirit of the German legal system. From this example, it can be seen that the sharing of partnership debts by shares has precedents in our country's legislation for reference. The reason why our association jointly petitioned last year was not without basis. Up to this point, it cannot be supplemented again. This is the first point. (2) From the perspective of procedural law for legislation, commercial registration belonged to commercial registration during the era of the Beijing government. The legislation of the Beijing government was originally based on the precedents compiled by the Law Compilation Institute of the former Qing Dynasty, separating the civil and commercial laws. Therefore, Regarding Commercial Registration (i.e., commercial registration), the third chapter of the Merchants' General Provisions, which was promulgated by the former Beijing government on March 2, 1914, and implemented on September 1 of the same year, already had detailed regulations. After the establishment of the National Government, this code of law did not conflict with the Party's laws and regulations, so it could still be used. Although there were very few legal provisions for commercial registration in the Merchants' General Provisions, there were clear regulations that each merchant should report registration to the relevant government office in the location of its business. Now, although the Legislative Yuan has combined the civil and commercial laws into one compilation in legislation, the legislation on commercial registration is still like the various parts of the Company Law, Insurance Law, Negotiable Instruments Law, and Maritime Law, and they must still be kept independent. The importance of the commercial registration law can be seen from this article. Moreover, Shanghai is the center of national commerce and the hub of trade with foreign countries. Commercial registration is extremely important. Moreover, partnership business in commerce, except for merchants with independent capital and company organizations, all belong to partnership business. Its importance in commerce is self-evident. Moreover, the term 'relevant government office in the location of the business' for the registration agency is somewhat vague. Instead, merchants in partnership business should first request registration from the city or county chamber of commerce in the location of the business, and then the chamber of commerce should report it to the local judicial authority and the central administrative agency on a monthly or quarterly basis for careful recording. In the current chamber of commerce system, the chamber of commerce is the general assembly of commercial groups. The so-called commercial groups are molecular organizations formed by the local trade associations. Therefore, in the future, all commercial registration should first be reported by each Merchant to its trade association, then the trade association should report to the county and city chamber of commerce, and then the county and city chamber of commerce should report to the local judicial authority and the local and central administrative agencies (i.e., the Ministry of Industry) on a monthly or quarterly basis. The county and city chambers of commerce, in addition to reporting according to law, should also make public announcements in their official gazettes for promulgating regulations on a monthly or quarterly basis. In this way, the parts are classified and clearly listed. Regardless of the capital of the partnership, the names of the partners, and the brand and address of the partnership business, there is reliable evidence for reference. If the partnership business fails and the partnership property is insufficient to pay off the debtors, each partner should naturally share the damaged debt amount on a pro rata basis, not only allowing creditors to know the actual situation of the partnership business at any time and place, but also each partner will have no excuse to shirk the obligations they bear, and there is no need for further investigation or evidence when the judicial authority makes a judgment. This is what is legally called being able to resist bona fide third parties because of registration (i.e., creditors). On the contrary, if a partnership business is not registered in accordance with current laws, and the partnership business fails and the partnership property is insufficient to pay off the debts, regardless of the amount and value of the investment of the partnership, any creditor can demand joint and several liability from any investor in the partnership, regardless of the total amount of their shares. This is what is called not being able to resist bona fide third parties because of non-registration (i.e., creditors). If the provisions of Article 681 of the current Civil Code are applied to this, it can be said that there is absolutely no doubt.

Based on the above discussion, in terms of substantive laws and regulations, the history of joint liability and pro rata sharing of partnership businesses in our country's legislation is not without consideration. In terms of continuing laws and regulations, the commercial registration law, if strictly formulated according to the above procedures, is to protect the safety of commerce and the consolidation of creditor's rights. Regardless of whether the current legislative purpose is to protect creditor's rights or protect debtor's rights, it is necessary to enforce compulsory registration and encourage the implementation of contract laws and regulations. Even if partnership businesses do not request registration, they should be subject to Appropriate penalties will prevent future partnership organizations from being frightened by the provisions of Article 681 of the Civil Code and seek dissolution, as today's commerce is unstable. On the positive side, precisely because of this Civil Code Article 68, and the enactment of mandatory regulations for commercial registration, it can safely engage in legitimate commerce, so that its business can be consolidated and its credit can be long-term. Progress, We, the association, respectfully present our humble opinions in two respects. We respectfully request that your esteemed association forward them to the members of the Legislative Yuan for adoption, for which we will be infinitely grateful. Sincerely, Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Shanghai Municipal Grain, Oil Cake Industry Association, Shanghai Municipal Head Rice Industry Association."

Municipal Government Responds to Chamber of Commerce

Land Transfer Fees Difficult to Reduce 131

The Municipal Chamber of Commerce previously presented a petition to the Municipal Government based on the resolutions of the Fifth General Assembly of Members, requesting that the tax rate for real estate transfer taxes levied by the city be reduced to 3.6%, in order to reduce the burden on citizens. Now, it has received a reply from the Municipal Government stating: "Received your presentation and instructed the Land Bureau to reply. The Land Bureau replied that real estate transfers within the city area that have not undergone the exchange of land permits will be subject to a 1% handling fee at the time of contract signing, previously called municipal expenses, and 5% was paid. Later, in order to reduce the burden on owners, it was requested to change it to a 1% handling fee and a land guarantee stamp fee. After the land certificate is exchanged, all transfers only require an 8% transfer tax, which is 8.4%, which is slightly lower than the contract signing. Within the land value tax area, it is reduced to 2.1%. In the future, after the land value tax is widespread, this transfer tax will also be reduced accordingly. Furthermore, the transfer tax rate in this city is nominally higher than 6.3%, but in terms of the same contract transfer, for example, in Baoshan County, which is adjacent to this city, all real estate transfers must pay an autonomous fee of 8% of the contract value, plus a 6% contract tax, totaling 14%. In addition, there are special construction donations and fundraising expenses, which are not included. Now, in this city, the 8% tax payment includes all transfer fees and the 1% handling fee, totaling only 9%. The burden is already significantly different. Since this city started levying land value tax, this income has been greatly reduced. If the transfer tax in areas where land value tax has not been levied is reduced to 6.3%, tax revenue will be even more reduced. After receiving the order, a bureau affairs meeting was convened for detailed discussion. It was generally believed that the land transfer in the temporary land value tax area of this city is subject to a 2% transfer tax, which is lower than the 6.3% method decided by the financial meeting. Therefore, the chamber of commerce's request to reduce the tax rate is difficult to handle, and it is intended to continue to handle the transfer tax rate according to the old regulations. In addition to ordering that it be handled according to the established regulations, it is hereby notified for your information." This is the reply.

Ewo Yusheng Ship

Replacement of Comprador Dispute Resolved 133

Negotiation Results from Union Introduction

Xu, the comprador of the Nanhua class Yusheng ship of Jardine Matheson, passed away due to illness, and a Mr. Feng was appointed by the Hong Kong head office to take over. Unexpectedly, after Mr. Feng took over, he brought 30 workers from Hong Kong, intending to replace all the original cargo handling workers on the ship, which caused a dispute. This case has been going on for a month. Initially, the Jardine Matheson Club negotiated without success. Later, it was submitted to the Chinese Seamen's Union for handling. Secretary Sun Luping was dispatched to negotiate directly with the company. Mr. Tudor, the general manager of the company, respects the union and has no objection, but due to long-standing practices, the cargo handling workers have always been hired by the comprador, so it is not convenient to interfere. Later, in order to take care of the livelihoods of the workers, the union was allowed to introduce candidates for the position of comprador on the ship, or directly appoint a worker to fill the position. As for the deposit, due to the union's involvement, the original amount of 5,000 yuan is now only 2,000 yuan, which will allow the company to dismiss the newly appointed comprador Feng to resolve the dispute. Otherwise, the comprador has the right to hire workers, and the company has no way to guarantee it. It is now known that the union has introduced Shi Yonggao, the comprador of the ship, to be promoted to comprador based on the wishes of the workers. All cargo handling workers continue to work as usual, and the contract was finalized yesterday. All 30 workers brought by Mr. Feng left the ship that day. According to the union's introduction, the comprador has always been the company's used Shan gong. This has never been seen before. This move has created a new record in the shipping industry and has set a precedent for breaking the contracting system.

Public Concession

Fire Fighting Equipment is Becoming More and More Perfect 138

A New Ladder Ordered from Germany

Can Rescue People from High-Rise Fires

丨Even the Smallest Lane Can Be Driven into for Rescue丨

The Shanghai Times reported that Shanghai is becoming more and more prosperous, and the new houses built are very high. Whenever a fire occurs, there are many dangers. Therefore, the fire brigade of the Public Concession recently ordered a new ladder from Germany. This is the second ladder of this type in the whole community. It has now been shipped to the Hongkou police station, where engineer Bao Wei is supervising the assembly. The ladder is 150 feet high and can accommodate two people carrying belts to climb to the top. If someone is trapped in a burning house, they can be rescued with this ladder. The ladder is raised and lowered by a mechanism, which is extremely agile. It is mounted on a copper car with a speed of up to 55 miles per hour. Another special feature is that it can be driven into small lanes. It is said that it can be used at the end of this month.

Four Major Oil Companies Cooperate

Gasoline Prices Rise Again 139

Rises Up to Five Corners Per Ten Gallons

Kerosene Imports Soar

Since the United Kingdom, the United States, and Russia agreed to stop competing and selling in order to recover previous losses, kerosene prices in our country's kerosene market have been rising. Recently, prices have been increased uniformly, and each country is trying its best to export and dump excess kerosene to China. As a result, the import volume in June of this year has increased sharply. The details are as follows:

Gasoline Prices Rise According to people in the gasoline industry, since the four major petroleum companies, Asia, Mobil, Texaco, and Oil Land, agreed to raise prices, prices have gradually increased. A month ago, the price per ten gallons was still 8.1 yuan, but the original price in this month was far less than the cost. In order to maintain business, it was decided to increase it by another five corners. The current price per ten gallons is 8.6 yuan, an increase of half a yuan. In the future, it is planned to continue to increase within a possible range.

Kerosene Imports Soar According to customs reports, the import volume of kerosene in my country in June of this year has increased sharply again. The imports from British North Borneo were 76 liters, worth the gold unit. Japan imported 303 liters, worth 27 gold units. The Dutch East Indies imported 7,139,652 liters, worth 297,995 gold units. The United States imported 2,922,22 liters, worth 140,687 gold units. The Soviet Union imported 12,526,618 liters from European ports, worth 501,065 gold units. Other countries imported 1,177 liters, worth 190 gold units. Excluding the number of foreign destinations, the total is 21,920,708 liters, worth 885,330 gold units, an increase of 19,689,309 liters over the import volume in May, an increase of 749,305 gold units in value.

Scorching Sun

Fire in Yangjiadu 141

Dozens of People Homeless

Public Security Bureau Will Provide Relief

The house of Ci Liu, a woman from Taixing, No. 19 Diandang Lane, behind Yangjiadu Street in Pudong, suddenly caught fire at about 12:30 yesterday afternoon. The fire broke through the roof immediately. At that time, the sun was scorching and the weather was extremely hot, and the fire became more intense. Ci Liu was panicked because her husband was working outside. Yang Chang, who learned about the fire from the First Branch of the Third District, immediately ordered Second Patrolman Sun Bu and Police Chief Dai to lead the police to suppress the fire. The police first used wooden buckets to draw water from nearby to put out the fire. Soon, the Pudong Fire Brigade also drove to the scene. At the same time, Yuanyi Stack in the west and Yingchang Factory in the north also drove pump cars to help. Because the distance from the Yangtze River was far, they could only rely on the well in the nearby goldfish pond and the dyeing workshop for water supply, so it was difficult to put out the fire for a while. After burning for about half an hour, it spread to three neighboring houses, and the front and back of a small restaurant opened by Chen, a woman from Jiangbei, No. 220 Yangjiadu Street behind. At this time, the firefighters worked hard to put out the fire and gradually extinguished it, and it did not spread further. In total, seven bungalows were destroyed. In addition to the small restaurant occupying three rooms, there were four other rooms, inhabited by ten households, all poor people from other provinces, with dozens of people of all ages. They were homeless and in a very pitiful state. After the fire was extinguished, the police at the post took Ci Liu, who started the fire, to the police station. She claimed that she was out to buy soap when the fire started, and it was probably caused by the fire not being extinguished after the meal. Director Yang ordered her to be sent to the bureau for punishment, and also asked the headquarters to find ways to help the victims of the fire.

Robbery on Shanhai Pass Road

Police Arrest a Bandit 142

Bandit Fired Guns and Fled

Finally Shot Down and Captured

At about 5:00 p.m. yesterday, six bandits suddenly came to a certain tobacco shop at No. 560, the intersection of Shanhai Pass Road and Datong Road. They were wearing black and white short shirts and pants, and two of them were hiding pistols. One bandit was guarding outside, and the rest of the bandits broke into the shop and shouted at the shop owner, shop assistant, and apprentice, forbidding them to make a sound. They forced them to hand over the key to the money cabinet, opened the cabinet, and robbed all the cash and foreign currency worth about 130 yuan stored inside. When the bandits saw that their goal had been achieved, they hurried out to escape. Before long after the bandits left the door, the shop assistant also followed out. The bandits did not notice and followed all the way until the intersection of Meibaige Road and Baike Road. The shop assistant saw the bandits were dividing the spoils and trying to flee in all directions, so he urgently reported to the police at the post and led them to identify and arrest the bandits. Unexpectedly, the bandits were discovered, and when the police arrived, they had fled in all directions. One of the bandits continued to flee along Baike Road. The police blew their whistles and bravely chased after him. The bandit was in a hurry and fired a gun at the police. The police also fired back. The bandit fought and fled until he reached the entrance of the Baolong Hospital, where he was finally shot down by the police and his pistol was seized. The police immediately reported to the Xinzha police station by telephone and sent a car to take the bandit to the Public Concession Hospital. At the same time, they chased and arrested the other fugitives and will investigate the case and bring them to justice.

Illegitimate Son Does Not Engage in Honest Work

Threatening Letter to Foster Father 143

Demanding 50 Yuan with a Deadline for Payment

Foster Father Reports to Police, Who Order a Warrant

Sun Xiechun Niugudian (牛骨店 - Ox Bone Shop) at No. 88 Baodai Lane, Xiaodongmen, is owned by Sun Maotang, a native of Ningbo, and has been in business for over 30 years. In 1919, Sun, through a friend's introduction, adopted a five-month-old child, naming him Sun Derong (also known as Defu), who is now 22 years old. Later, Sun's wife also gave birth to two sons, aged 12 and 7. The family of five, including his wife, all reside in the shop, relying entirely on business income. They live frugally and are able to maintain a warm and adequately fed life. He once instructed his adopted son, Derong, to learn a trade at a machinery factory and even helped him get married. Unexpectedly, this adopted son does not engage in honest work, but willingly sinks into degradation. Despite his foster father's repeated admonitions, his bad habits are deeply ingrained, and he consistently refuses to change. Recently, he even secretly engraved a seal, defrauding various places of goods to convert them into cash for his use. Not content with this, he also sent threatening letters to Sun's relatives, demanding money and spending it like water. A few days ago, he had another fantastic idea. He sent a letter through the post office to his foster father, Sun Maotang, with threatening content, demanding 50 yuan and setting a three-day deadline to deliver the money to the tea room outside the third-floor hall of the Dongfang Hotel in Xiaodongmen. Otherwise, it said, unexpected things would happen. After receiving the letter, Sun felt that his adopted son not only showed no respect for his elders, but also had completely forgotten the 20 years of nurturing he had received. Therefore, in addition to commissioning a lawyer to publish a statement in the newspaper severing their father-son relationship, he also reported the original threatening letter and all the bad deeds to Liu Yunfang, the director of the second section of the first district of the Municipal Public Security Bureau, who immediately ordered his subordinates to arrest his son, Sun Derong, for interrogation and subsequent punishment.

Female School Teacher

Rescuing an Abused Maid 144

Reported by the Ciyouhui (慈幼會 - Child Welfare Association), Transferred to the Police Station

The Maid is Temporarily Sent to the Jiliang Institute (濟良所 - Institute for Rescuing Women) After Interrogation

Li Jieshun, a girl from Suqian, Jiangbei, is currently 17 years old. Since childhood, due to poverty, her parents sold her to Chen Yangwen, a native of Anhui, as a maid for 60 yuan. Chen is a tea merchant who lives with his family at No. 36, Lane 646, Tiantong Road. However, since Li came to Chen's house as a maid, for more than ten years, she has been subjected to abuse by Chen's wife, Wen, who often mistreats her and whips her at every turn. This was seen by Zhu Desi, a teacher at the nearby Zhonghua Girls' School, who felt great pity. She then wrote a letter to the Zhonghua Ciyouhui, describing everything in detail. Zhao Jian, a clerk of the association, secretly investigated and confirmed the facts, and immediately reported to the Huishi Police Station. The police station sent Detective Shang Wu and Bao Detective Ke Zhang to bring Li to the police station at 7 p.m. the day before yesterday. After transferring her to Guangren Hospital for examination and injuries, she was temporarily sent to the Jiliang Institute for shelter. Yesterday morning, the institute sent the girl to the Fifth Criminal Court of the First Special Court for instructions. Jiang Baolian, the police station's lawyer, then presented the case, stating that Chen Yangwen, the girl's master, was not in Shanghai, so the police station had summoned Chen Wen, the mistress, for questioning yesterday. According to Mrs. Chen, she had scolded and beaten Li the day before because Li had gone to the barber shop to have her hair trimmed, and Li insisted that the mistress go with her, which led to an argument. However, Li's conduct on weekdays was poor, and she often spoke insolently to the mistress, resulting in the beatings. Yesterday, the police station sent Li to Guangren Hospital, which confirmed that she had minor injuries on her left arm and right leg. Now, Chen Wen and all the witnesses have turned themselves in and requested a hearing. Li Jieshun stated that she was 17 years old, and her parents used to be in Jiangbei. She was sold to the Chen family as a maid at the age of four and has been repeatedly abused and beaten. A few days ago, Teacher Zhu saw that she was pitiful and offered help. Now, she does not want to go back with the mistress, nor does she want to sue her. She wants to go to the Jiliang Institute to study. Zhu Desi, a teacher at the Zhonghua Girls' School, testified that she reported to the Ciyouhui because she saw Chen Wen repeatedly abusing the girl. When Chen Wen was questioned, she admitted that she had spent 60 yuan to buy Li as an adopted daughter more than ten years ago, but denied abuse. Judge Deng Baosun reviewed the confession and ordered Li Jieshun to be temporarily placed in the Jiliang Institute.

After Rehearing the Assassination Case in Yinghua Lane

Chen Bingquan Found Not Guilty 145

If the Police Abandon the Appeal

Chen Can Immediately Regain His Freedom

On December 15, 1928, an assassination case occurred in Yinghua Lane, Roberts Road, West Shanghai. At that time, Chen Hongyu (also known as Xiaoxing) was shot and killed. The police subsequently arrested the perpetrators, Pan Qifang and Chen Bingquan, and sent them to the First Special Court. After interrogation, Pan was sentenced to death and is currently detained in prison, awaiting approval from higher authorities for execution. Chen Bingquan was sentenced to life imprisonment. Chen was dissatisfied with the judgment and appealed to the Second Branch Court, but his appeal was rejected. However, Chen Bingquan's wife, believing that her husband had been wrongly accused, hired lawyer Chen Tingrui to appeal to the Supreme Court. After review, the Supreme Court found that there were still doubts in the case and sent it back to the Second Branch Court for a retrial. The retrial concluded on the 26th of last month. The day before yesterday morning, Presiding Judge Yu announced the judgment. The main text read, "The original judgment is revoked, and Chen Bingquan is declared not guilty." However, Wang Yaotang, the police station's lawyer, stated that the police station still needed to consider whether to appeal Chen Bingquan and requested permission to remand him in custody, which the court granted. If the police abandon the appeal, Chen can be released. Therefore, Chen's acquittal this time is entirely due to the efforts of Chen's lawyer.

The details are as follows:

Provincial Troops Headed Upstream

Since receiving reports of bandits at Baisha Shuikou, the Fujian provincial military and political authorities loaded troops and sailed upstream from Sanduao on the 2nd. The provincial army is currently advancing to pursue and suppress the bandits. The market in Fuzhou is as usual, and the people are very stable.

Merchant Ships Sail as Usual

Japanese People's Stories Exaggerated

There are not many Japanese people in Fuzhou, but there are quite a few Taiwanese people. This time, they used the excuse of bandits to exaggerate the stories. However, yesterday, the Fuzhou gang received a telegram from the Hakka saying that the provincial capital was stable, and the Fujian provincial government was even more serious about protecting foreigners. The public security is stable, and all industries are still trading as usual. There is no panic at all.

Bloodshed in a Mahjong Game 148

Chen Tian's Consciousness Confused

Fu Shuangfu Detained Pending Investigation

Chen Tian, a woman from Zhenjiang, 32 years old, lives at Zhongxin Road, Zhaogu Road, in the city. At around 8 p.m. the day before yesterday, she was playing the game of "Fangcheng" (mahjong) with Fu Shuangfu, who owns a coal shop next door, and others, with 500 points per small game. Because Fu discarded a "9 of Bamboo", the next player happened to be waiting for a "6 and 9 of Bamboo" to complete a pure suit with three sets. Chen was not convinced, arguing that Fu should not have discarded the "9 of Bamboo" because the next player had already declared three "筒子" (bamboo suit) tiles. A heated argument ensued. Unexpectedly, Fu Shuangfu was unwilling to be outdone and retorted with barbed words. Chen became enraged and accused Fu of speaking rudely. She rushed forward, grabbed him, and slapped his face. Fu struggled free and grabbed a cup, throwing it violently. It hit Chen Tian's forehead, causing her head to bleed immediately and breaking two blood vessels above her eyebrows. She lost a lot of blood and fainted to the ground. People who saw this were shocked and alarmed. They realized that Fu Shuangfu had caused the trouble and quickly called the police, who arrested Fu Shuangfu and took him to the second section of the second district for interrogation. The injured person was sent to Qu Zhibu Hospital for treatment. The doctor found that the injury was not minor and quickly used medicine to seal and bandage it. Yesterday morning, Police Chief Gao from the police station sent the accused to the local court for investigation. Police Chief Gao requested an early hearing because Chen Tian was unconscious and there was a fear that her life was in danger. Early treatment might save her. Heeding the instruction, the prosecutor opened a court session and found that Chen Tian was seriously injured. He ordered her to be sent to the hospital for treatment, and Fu Shuangfu was detained pending further instructions.

Cigarette and Tobacco Industry Association

Discussion on Methods for Increasing License Donations 149

The Shanghai Cigarette and Tobacco Industry Association previously received a request from members such as Ding Ruitai of Laobaidu Street, stating that the original license donation of 2 yuan was now to be increased to 20 yuan, and the others were to be increased to 4, 8, or 12 yuan. They requested the association to seek relief measures. The association invited representatives from the industry north and south of Shanghai the day before yesterday to hold a meeting to discuss the measures, which were reported in the previous newspaper. Yesterday, the members from the southern city went to the office in the south of Shanghai and continued to hold a discussion meeting at 3 p.m. Many people attended, and Chai Yasheng was elected as the chairman to report on the progress of the meeting in recent days. Then, Qian Xuanqing and other members of Yongkang Company reported that they had read in yesterday's newspaper that the Finance Bureau's talk about the license tax must be collected in accordance with the regulations, expressing determination to regard tobacco and alcohol products as consumables with anesthetic and toxic properties, which would harm society and should be banned or heavily taxed to increase the selling price so that people would no longer buy them. Local social morals could be clarified. Now, the Finance Bureau intends to ban consumable and anesthetic tobacco and alcohol products and increase taxes heavily to increase their selling prices so that people will not be harmed by the poison. Its intention is very good, but Shanghai's tobacco and alcohol merchants should not bear the burden alone. Other ports have not yet implemented this. It is too inconsiderate of the livelihoods of Shanghai's tobacco and alcohol merchants. It is inappropriate compared to the resolution of the All-Financial Conference. However, the licenses previously obtained by our industry were to pay the tax on domestic tobacco. Now, the domestic tobacco in this city has disappeared. We have no choice but to also operate cigarettes, but the profit is very small. Daily life is still difficult to maintain. The cigarette licenses should be included in the consolidated tax in the 20th year, and a separate cigarette shop license should be sold, which should be exempt. Now, not only are they not exempt, but they are also heavily taxed, which is also inappropriate. If you must increase the tax, it should be added to the consolidated tax so that the burden on merchants is not increased, the government's tax revenue is sufficient, and the people's livelihoods are maintained. If the Finance Bureau regards tobacco and alcohol as harmful to society, it should petition the central government to order the national administrative organs to strictly investigate, prohibit, and ban them. It should not increase the taxes heavily, creating a new record for Shanghai's tobacco and alcohol merchants. If the selling prices of tobacco and alcohol in the Chinese area of this city are increased, cutting off the customers, will it make the concession prosper and put the Chinese industry to death? The authorities should be asked to consider whether this is in line with the meaning of the late Mr. Sun Yat-sen. Subsequently, Qian Wenda, Chen Enqi, Wang Bingzhong, and others successively proposed three measures: (1) If members in the southern city are forced to pay heavy taxes after applying for registration or obtaining licenses, they should prepare a letter and send it to this office, which will be forwarded to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to request correction and reduction to show fairness. (2) If there is oppressive behavior, the final course of action will be determined. (3) A draft will be submitted to the executive committee to issue a declaration. The meeting was adjourned.

Domestic Matches

Sales Unimpeded After Price Increase 150

The Shanghai match industry was almost unsustainable due to being restricted by foreign goods dumping and running at a loss. Later, after the Ministry of Finance issued a new tariff rate for imported goods, it was able to inhibit dumping slightly. However, the cost of raw materials and labor is expensive. Since the price cut, it has not recovered. The match industry could not bear it for long, so it specially convened six provinces in Shanghai in May to form a match industry maintenance association and agreed to increase the price of each box by 1 to 5 or 6 yuan to maintain capital. This was approved by the Ministry of Finance. Yesterday, people in the match industry said that sales had not been affected much after the price increase. Also, the match industry association previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance to set up a control committee to determine the entire rescue plan for the match industry. The Ministry of Finance has agreed to its request.

Extortionist Cao Shifang Sentenced 163

Cao Shifang, a local resident, lived at No. 132 Taopeng Road. Initially, due to an unclear address, five letters were mistakenly sent to No. 190 in the same neighborhood to Zhang Tongjun, a Ningbo native who worked as a bookkeeper at the Ewo Cotton Mill. During the adjourned investigation, it was found that the defendant had written similar letters between January 5th and March 27th of this year and sent them to Cai Yousheng at No. 5 Jixiang Lane, Dongxi Huade Road, and to the monk Song Hanjiang (a doctor of salty business) at No. 27 Fenzhou Road, extorting silver dollars, otherwise threatening them with bombs and pistols. Subsequently, the plaintiffs and representatives Fei Huilin and Xu Wushan testified about the situation at the time and questioned the defendant, who admitted everything without denial and asked for leniency. Judge Xiao sentenced Cao Shifang to six years in prison. The number of days in detention before the judgment was finalized will be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day of imprisonment. The threatening letters were confiscated.

The China Jisheng Society received letters from Chen Yici, Zhu Liangting, Gu Youmin, and Xu Maozhao, gentlemen of Haiyan County, Zhejiang Province, stating that since the beginning of summer, the weather has been severely dry, and 80 to 90 percent of the rice seedlings have withered and died. Mr. Zhou Yangsong, a representative of the society, held a letter requesting relief. According to a telegram from Li Dexing and others of the Drought Relief Committee of Taihu County, Anhui Province, Tai County has suffered a long drought without rain, and the autumn crops are hopeless. Those who survive banditry are also victims of a disastrous year. The cries of the starving are everywhere, and there are tens of thousands of disaster-stricken households, begging for urgent relief. According to a telegram from Quan Jiao County, Anhui Province, since the great flood of the 20th year, the vitality has not recovered. This spring, there was another hailstorm, which reduced the harvest of the two wheats. Now, they are suffering from a drought, the rural areas are collapsing, nine out of ten households are empty, and they are selling their children and migrating. The suffering is unspeakable, and they are waiting for relief to survive. According to this, in recent years, floods and droughts have occurred frequently, and relief efforts are overwhelming. Now, Zhejiang and Anhui are reporting disasters, and the remaining hungry people are waiting for rescue. The association has already provided relief to Chang'an, Shaanxi, and Yingshang, Taihe, and Fuyang counties in Anhui this year, and the funds are insufficient, making it difficult to continue. It is hoped that charitable colleagues at home and abroad will donate money to save a life, which is better than building a seven-story pagoda, and the merits and virtues are immeasurable.

Hepingfang, Dongbaoxing Road, Zhabei, organized the Fourth Branch of the Shanghai Rent Reduction Committee in Zhabei District to participate in the rent reduction movement. Therefore, on the one hand, they filed a counterclaim against the owner and the manager in the original court to reduce the rent, and on the other hand, they unanimously participated in the rent arrears lawsuit. It is heard that during the second summons of the rent arrears case, all the tenants unanimously appeared in court. The rent reduction case has also been heard twice, but the defendant owner and the manager have not appeared in court. The rent in this Fang is particularly expensive compared to other places because the owner took advantage of the chaos after the war by the British merchant Wuhe Foreign Firm's management department, and after a slight repair, they took the opportunity to double the rent. The tenants of the Fang have endured hardships and persevered until now. Due to the impact of the recession, life has become increasingly difficult. They have repeatedly sent letters to the owner and the management department, asking them to understand the difficulties and reduce the rent, but they have not received a reply. Representatives were sent to them, but they avoided meeting them. Instead, Wuhe Foreign Firm sued 42 households in the Fang for rent arrears. All the oppression suffered by the Fang prompted them to resist. It is heard that the reasons for demanding rent reduction are quite sufficient. The organization of the association is very sound. The committee must hold meetings twice a week, with no absences. The proposals of the committee members are carefully considered, and the overall unity is very strong. They unanimously refuse to pay rent and store the money in the bank in order to achieve the goal of rent reduction.

Reader Q&A

How to Watch Movies (Continued) 176

Chinese movies, without exception, are supporters of a particular social class, because the right to produce them is also controlled by the hands of a particular social class. Initially, films like "Burning of the Red Lotus Temple" appeared. The role of these films was clearly to use the influence of legendary novels to more widely implement anesthesia, causing the masses to obediently return to the embrace of the martial arts heroes produced by feudal society, letting the heroes "eliminate violence" for them, letting the heroes "pacify the people," in order to eliminate the masses' struggle for their own survival. However, this kind of effect is the easiest to expose. When the masses in deep water and dire straits never see so-called heroes come to save them, then those superb skills of flying over walls and walking on eaves finally become only illusions in their minds. Therefore, what followed was the production of distorted love movies. Chinese love movies are often different from European and American love movies. European and American love movies completely use the stimulation of flesh and gorgeous sets to eliminate anger towards life, but Chinese love movies are not like this. Their main content mostly describes a woman who falls in love because she is tempted by material things and seduced by men. The result is either being abused or abandoned by the man, or pulling back from the brink, finally awakening and completing the satisfactory return of lovers becoming family. Of course, the effect of this kind of film is much more effective than martial arts films. Undoubtedly, it has temporarily satisfied some backward elements, and won them a sigh of sympathy, but this is only a sigh of sympathy after all, only temporary satisfaction. Therefore, these clever gentlemen must once again further implement their clever schemes from another aspect. Recent films such as "Sister Flowers," "Song of the Fishermen," as well as "The Wild History of Yao Mountain," and "Mr. Wang," are products that achieve their ultimate goals through various different expressions. Films such as "The Wild History of Yao Mountain" and "Mr. Wang," the former uses an adventurous and bizarre story, while the latter is purely a boring and ridiculous story. These films, whether in content or form, are actually "Burning of the Red Lotus Temple" with a changed face. Here, we want to specifically mention "Sister Flowers" and "Song of the Fishermen." They are currently the most attractive films to the audience. In "Sister Flowers," Da Bao and Er Bao, sisters from the same background, one due to her outstanding beauty, gains the favor of a general and even climbs to the position of wife, while the other, due to her unattractive appearance, is forever trapped in a life of hardship, and even becomes a prisoner. This contrast already contains the effect of "everything is fate," not to mention that the author imagines a very accidental reunion in the ending, completing the great happy ending of "one person achieves enlightenment, even his dogs and chickens rise to heaven." To be honest, "Sister Flowers" is comparable to "Laughing Destiny."

The above is the complete picture of the colorful Chinese film industry. If you want to gain any nourishment from it, it is very difficult. On the one hand, movies are supporters of a particular social class, but on the other hand, they must have an audience to support them. For business reasons, they must cater to the market. Therefore, only the power of the audience can promote the production of mass films.

Free Talk

I Come From The East (XIV)

— Hoshino

The most ridiculous were the three Filipinos on the ship. One was a professor of engineering at the University of the Philippines, and the other two were students at the University of Chicago. The professor was very prejudiced, thinking that everything in the Philippines was the best in the world. He said that his own daughter was more beautiful than any Hollywood actress. He also said that when he went to the United States, in every city, there were young American girls who admired his appearance and pursued him. One of the University of Chicago students immediately mocked him, saying that he was bragging because he was fancied by a pheasant. They started arguing. For more than ten days, they were in the same cabin and at the same table, but they didn't greet each other. The engineering professor, to ridicule the student, specially invited another University of Chicago student to live in his home after the ship arrived in Manila. Every time the professor talked to us, mentioning the advantages of the Philippines, the student would make jokes and harsh criticisms to us. The professor was a rough and dark brute. Everyone called him a boxer to his face, and secretly we regarded him as a bandit. The University of Chicago student was a thin and yellow youth, probably too romantic in the lower-class places in Chicago. His appearance was like a Shanghai gangster.

On the ship, we also met two sisters from Hong Kong. They boarded the ship from Hawaii. The older sister had a bit of seasickness and often stayed in bed, but the younger sister was not afraid of the wind and waves. On warm and sunny afternoons, the highest deck of the ship, quiet and bright, became the best place for us to talk and play games. We often played ping-pong, forgetting the time for meals. Both sisters had a good foundation and deep interest in Chinese literature. When we talked about Song poetry and Yuan opera, sometimes we laughed heartily, and sometimes we suddenly seemed to understand something. The older sister could dance the graceful Hawaiian hula, and the younger sister could sing Hawaiian songs and play the piano. There was nothing to do on the ship, and enjoying the beautiful music and dance, we unconsciously felt as if a second free and happy Hawaii had appeared in the Pacific Ocean.

On the eve of the ship's arrival in Shanghai, we leaned on the railing as usual. The cool sea breeze made our hair messy. The black night sky was full of stars, and they were describing the beautiful scenery of a clear night in Hawaii. I felt that their words were very poetic, and the younger sister was also very good at Chinese painting. No wonder her descriptions were very vivid. It was a pity that they couldn't speak Mandarin, and I couldn't speak Cantonese, so we used English instead. The sea was black in the deep night. As the steamship passed, it dragged a white snow wave behind it. We quietly looked at the nearing end of our journey, and everyone felt a nameless sense of melancholy.

What I Saw in Tokyo 177

On Pacific mail ships, except for Japanese ships, the sailors are all Chinese. The so-called Chinese refers to people from Guangdong, or several counties such as Taishan in Guangdong. Their possession of today's advantages is not because of skills or strength, but because they can accept the lowest wages. According to the Chinese sailors on the ship, they each get twenty-five Hong Kong dollars per month, and because of this little salary, they risk their lives in the ships of the Pacific. Of course, I don't know how many more Chinese people in the country accept even lower wages, with working environments that are worse and more bitter than on the ship, and are treated even more cruelly by their employers. But I often look at those Chinese crew members in white short shirts and blue long pants, those Chinese youths living under the yelling and scolding commands and attitudes of foreigners, and some of them are really very healthy and have very clear minds, and I feel very uncomfortable in my heart. I feel that they should not be working here.

Two Different Opinions from Mr. Wu Zhihui 178

— Xu Maoyong

It is gratifying that Mr. Wu Zhihui has also come to participate in the discussion of the mass language. Mr. Wu has not expressed his opinions on academic issues for a long time, but from this letter to Mr. Cao Juren, we can see that he has been paying attention to the issue of "mass language" from the beginning. Although the opinions expressed are somewhat vague in some places, they have indeed been carefully considered and are not just perfunctory. Therefore, these opinions are very noteworthy and worthy of discussion.

Mr. Wu also agrees with the establishment of a mass language, which will dispel the confusion of many people. Although it is a very small minority, there are still people who express doubt about the mass language, or say: "What exactly is the mass language?" or say: "The mass language is fundamentally wrong." For these people, a few words from Mr. Wu are enough to deal with them: "Classical Chinese, vernacular Chinese, and mass language have differences in ease of widespread adoption. Of course, vernacular Chinese is easier to be widely adopted than classical Chinese, and mass language will definitely be easier to be widely adopted than vernacular Chinese." To put it simply: the mass language is the most widespread language, which answers the question of "what exactly is the mass language." Vernacular Chinese is not widespread enough, and the mass language needs to be even more widespread. What could be wrong with that? However, if someone has a bit of a problem with their brain, they may still doubt "widespread": "Why must it be widespread?" Once it reaches this point, we can ignore them and let them doubt until they die! The mass language will henceforth be strongly demanded. Due to its "widespreadness," bookstores will demand mass language to compile books, because this will attract more readers. Film companies will demand mass language for explanations and dialogue, because this will attract more viewers. All propaganda and advertising agencies will also demand mass language for their use... The propositions and innovations of all scholars are not as powerful as actual needs, let alone the doubts and opposition of those with brain diseases.

If the mass language is established and is universally used by the masses, but the books compiled using this language and the movies explained still talk about poor people being beaten on the buttocks by the master and having to kowtow and thank him, and a young man and a young woman "doing clerkish" in the back garden... then the masses will still not watch it. As a result, the bookstore owner and the film company owner will still not be able to earn money. At that time, the "mass language" will still be negated.

This shows the importance of the issue of consciousness in the mass language issue. The so-called issue of consciousness is also the "defending the Way" issue that Wu Zhihui mentioned.

However, although Mr. Wu denies that literary style is related to defending the Way, I believe it is related.

For example, "Punishments do not extend to the high officials, rituals do not extend to the common people." These two sentences are classical Chinese that defends the Way, but they must not be translated into vernacular Chinese, let alone into mass language. The key lies entirely in the vagueness, or rather the beauty, of the words "punishments" and "rituals." The common people are foolish, but there is a limit to their foolishness. When they don't understand the meaning of what people are saying, they will foolishly believe it, but once they understand it, they will begin to doubt, and even become "angry." Therefore, the ancients established creeds, and the wording was always made as vague, general, abstract, and mysterious as possible, so that people would not understand it. This is what is meant by "fooling the people." Classical Chinese is suitable for the purpose of "fooling the people," so only classical Chinese can defend the Way without any flaws. Using vernacular Chinese can certainly write a "rituals do not extend to the common people" theory, but it will inevitably be too blunt and ultimately not good. If the purpose is to preach a doctrine or an ideology to the people, in order to make them understand, such as the Three Principles of the People, then it must be in vernacular Chinese. Classical Chinese can certainly write the Three Principles of the People, but it will never be as popular as vernacular Chinese. For an ideology to be universally understood and accepted, it must utilize a universal literary style. From this, we can see that literary style and defending the Way are indeed closely related, a point that Mr. Wu seems to have never considered.

I also have some different opinions on Mr. Wu's theory that "literature must die, and the great disaster will not stop." Mr. Wu's original intention was very good. He advocated using science and technology to relieve the masses, but he thought that literature and other knowledge were "harmful to your country and fierce to your family," so he advocated tearing it down. This intention was entirely for the country and for the masses. However, Mr. Wu thought things were too simple. He said, "If the mass language is unified, writing some simple science and technology articles" can "benefit the masses' rice bowls." Science and technology themselves have the potential to save the country and save the masses, but under the current circumstances, it is not possible. Just look at the United States. The language is unified, and science and technology are developed, but President Roosevelt is working hard on economic recovery, which shows that its national economy is declining. Its veterans and workers often riot and strike, which shows that not all of its masses have good rice bowls. Science and technology cannot save these situations. Is it entirely the fault of literature? This is generally not logical.

Mr. Wu meant that literature is entirely a trick played by intellectuals, and the masses do not need it now. Therefore, he said: "Wait until the loafers in the alleys need alley entertainment, and then let them create mass literature." This is also incorrect. The loafers in the alleys, the villagers in the fields, have always had everything, including literature, philosophy, and their own technology and science, fundamentally because they have all these needs. However, everything they currently have is low-level in terms of quality and poor in terms of quantity, and the masses of you and the masses of us are different from each other, not communicating and integrating, and therefore not changing and progressing. The establishment of the mass language is precisely to use the power of universal language to communicate and integrate the consciousness of all the masses of you and us, to enrich it, to change it, to make it progress, and to replace the original local and low-level everything with universal and high-level literature, philosophy, etc. The important thing here is still the purification of the consciousness of the masses. The psychology of the masses is the same as the psychology of the intellectuals. They are definitely not without other needs besides "rice bowls." Literature is also what they need. After the mass language is established, there will of course be mass language literature. (Moreover, in fact, the establishment of the mass language must first go through the attempt of mass language literature.) Mr. Wu has unfairly placed the responsibility for the "great disaster" on "literature," and it is even more incomprehensible to fundamentally deny literature. To support the mass language but deny mass language literature is to buy the casket and return the pearl.

Since the issue of establishing the mass language was established, I have fully agreed, but what I am researching is the technical issue of establishing the mass language and mass language literature, and I plan to write an article on one aspect. Now that I have seen Mr. Wu's paper, I feel that it is necessary to clarify the above two points, so I wrote this article first.

The Moon Lute (Continued) 179

— Li Qiao

The workers faithfully worked for the boss year in and year out. A kind of eager ambition to become nouveau riche sometimes makes them, after they receive their "monthly wages," regardless of whether their families are starving, bravely go to the gambling house to make a desperate gamble! But if they unfortunately fail, they will not regret it at all (thinking that the hard-earned price has been given to others for nothing). They still work hard. All-day fatigue, as well as sorrow for life, are wildly vented through various different actions and expressions in the evening after work.

Every night, I was so moved by Lao Zhang's moving moon lute sound. In the noisy kitchen, under the dim gas lamp, I lazily lay on a moldy straw mat that Lao Zhang used as a floor mat next to him. Lao Zhang leaned against the wall and leisurely and absentmindedly played his old moon lute. A kind of melancholy, passion, weeping, anger, and rebellious clear sound vibrated in the irritable and depressing air, and all the shouts and rude voices would be silent like death.

When he first plays, he always plays some affectionate love songs and passionate love tunes, such as "Riverside Tune" (5), "Seaweed Tune" (6)... Gradually, he also plays the accompaniment to "Three-Step Walk" (7), a rhythmic and melodic sound that stimulates everyone's ears, and people will clap their hands in rhythm with him, or even impulsively and unconsciously start to dance the "Walk" (8).

After playing so enthusiastically for a while, he waited until people felt a little tired, and then gently played the poignant and compelling:

In October, it is cold and bleak,

Write a letter home to my wife:

There is no change at home,

Sell some odd things at will.

Don't want Guangdong haos,

Hubei haos are more or less acceptable.

The gloomy sound leads the hearts of everyone who is suffering so sour, and tears unknowingly flow on the dirty cheeks, almost crying!

Reply to Mr. Wu Zhihui (Excerpt) 180

— Cao Juren

Mr. Zhihui: Recently, while compiling "A History of the Debate Between Classical and Vernacular Chinese," I reread the "Awakening," "Learning Lamp," "Yusi," "National Language," and "Modern Review" from the thirteenth and fourteenth years of the Republic of China, and I couldn't help but smile bitterly. "You can't teach an old dog new tricks." As Mr. Liu Bannong had to say, "Only the Chinese would be so hopeless, forever circling aimlessly on problems that are not problems." Mr. Wang Maozu was entangled with Chen Duxiu and Hu Shi in the "New Youth." He sang a duet with Zhang Shizhao in "Post-Jia Yin" as if it were a serious matter. This time, he is reviving and reviving with such great enthusiasm. (Omission) Although the matter is foolish, the heart is of course pitiful!

(Above omission) Mr. previously detailed Zhang Shizhao's psychology, saying that his kind of bird-willow writing was intended to be appreciated by the ruling party and to amaze the bureaucrats; that kind of "Chen Xian's son taught his son to flatter" and other "ruling party examinations" were nothing more than the result of admiring actor-writers. If his wife was not ashamed and wept in the courtyard, I would not believe that such a thing really exists in the world... This time, Mr. is particularly forgiving towards Mr. Wang and Mr. Liu, saying that they have "seven parts intention to save people, and three parts intention to defend the Way." He also said: "Mr. Wang, Mr. Liu and others have no preconceived ideas, they are sacrificing for others, not protecting themselves." I privately disagree a little. After Mr. Wang's theory of reviving classical Chinese was published in "Times Public Opinion," it was followed by a response of "The Naturalness and Inevitability of the Revival of Classical Chinese," and the old spells of world affairs and human hearts in "Jia Yin" magazine were chanted. The Nanjing correspondent of "Ta Kung Pao" said how the revival of classical Chinese had become a new trend... These clues tell us: Mr. Wang's advocacy of reviving classical Chinese... the younger brother's way out is secondary, taking advantage of the chaotic world to grab a topic to write slogans and paste slogans, without waiting for Freud to analyze it, one can see his lungs and liver. (Omission) I feel that the atmosphere of this revival of classical Chinese is too similar to the "tiger" atmosphere of the fourteenth year of the Republic of China, and we cannot forgive it!

The mass language issue should be "lowered without much high theory," and the masses should do it themselves. It is "self-evident" and beyond doubt. The current thing is that we must first persuade all our pen-holding friends to relax a little on the power of writing, so that everyone has a hand to move. When Mr. Hu Shi was in the United States, he spent a lot of effort to persuade Mei Guangdi, Ren Hongjun... and those friends to believe that living literature should be done in vernacular Chinese. At one time, Mei Guangdi also said, "The literary revolution should start with folk literature, which goes without saying, but it must go through a major war," and later, after returning to China, he acted as a bodyguard for classical Chinese in "Xue Heng." Pen-holding friends, no matter what, always feel that writing is precious and want to monopolize it and are unwilling to make it public to the masses. Knowing that phonetic alphabets, Roman alphabets, and simplified characters are all tools that are beneficial to the masses, they are deliberately put aside, and they are unwilling to learn them or teach them. I said last year, "Writing wrong characters doesn't matter," and I was scolded a lot. We must at least have the spirit of missionaries, going on again and again, without fear of trouble. I think: The old colleagues of the National Language Research Association must not relax this responsibility. The revolution has not yet succeeded, and comrades still need to work hard." This time, I made a foolish wish and wrote many letters, asking Hu Shi, Zhou Zuoren, Qian Xuantong, Li Jinxi, Fu Sinian, and Dian Yue... in Beijing and Lu Xun, Mao Dun, Sun Fuyuan, and Lu Yiyan... in Shanghai to express their opinions. For example, writing the Diamond Sutra, whether or not it can become a Buddha, let it go, but writing must be done one sheet at a time. Mr. is a founding elder of the national language movement, with "achievements hanging in the universe," and there are many practical things. Please Mr. express some more opinions!

Cao Juren respectfully replies

(Note) (1) Touzi Mine is the best mine. (2) The furnace room is the place where large furnaces are set up to smelt ore, like a general headquarters. Everything needed on the factory has to be prepared from here. (3) The boss is the owner. (4) The Guangdong gang refers to the Cantonese who do tin business there. Their capital is very strong and they can manipulate the tin price of Gejiu. (5) Riverside tune is a mountain song sung by people from Hexi. (6) Seaweed tune refers to the kind of mountain song sung by people from Shiping: the sound is very long and elegant. (7) Three-step walk is a kind of dance for peasant women. The method is to tiptoe, take three steps forward and three steps back, the posture is very beautiful. (8) Dancing the walk is like what civilized people call dancing. When dancing, there is the accompaniment of the moon lute and the crisp sound of the leather snuffbox, "tata," to help with excitement and rhythm.

Longing For 181

— Pu Feng

In the not-so-distant distance,

There is light shining.

Longing, grasping, pursuing,

Smash the shackles on the body,

Build sweet laughter.

The road is not far,

Don't worry:

Not a lone boat

Drifting in the sea,

Not a single horse alone

Galloping and leaping in the dark night.

Longing, longing...

There is light ahead to guide,

There is light ahead to shine!

The Setting Sun Still Lingers in the Human World 182

— Liu Shijun

I wander on the ancient ruins accompanied by a lonely, thin shadow, as if something occupies my mind, like the dark night occupying the world before dawn.

At this time, the undulating suburbs have long been dressed in bleak autumn clothes, and the haggard face appears even more haggard, like willows that are about to wither, like roses that have already withered, even more like the rouge on the lips of a dying girl. In the near, in the far, in the farther, one cannot see a single green grass, a single green leaf, a single red flower, only countless earthen mounds, silently waiting for partners to provide steamed bun fillings in the city.

No, there are...

There, one can also see desolate smoke and weeds, one can also see broken tablets and dilapidated monuments, one can also see cold crows and decaying willows: in addition, one can also see the scattered and horizontal defeated battlements, and the three or two collapsing thatched huts.

No, there are...

There, there are also hunchbacked old people, there are also haggard young people, there are also lonely children... they, are working and resting there; they, are sleeping and waking there; they, are singing and crying there; they, are living and dying there.

No, there is...

Oh! The setting sun still lingers in the human world.

1924, 7, 17, revised in West Lake.

Tianjin-Shanghai Interport Tennis Tournament Opens

Zheng Zhaojia Suffers Miserable Defeat 185

Erlong Qian Wins in Straight Sets

Little Zheng's Failure is a Great Surprise

One Singles and One Doubles Match Today

(Tianjin, 3rd Dispatch) The Tianjin-Shanghai Interport Tennis Tournament, the first day, was held at 5:00 PM today at the tennis court in the British Concession. Zheng Zhaojia and Erlong Qian, in the second singles match, Little Zheng was miserably defeated by Erlong Qian in straight sets. The match ended at 6:00 PM. The doubles match will be held at 3:00 PM on the 4th. After appearing on the court today, Little Zheng was quite loved by more than a thousand spectators. Because Little Zheng was agile, and Erlong Qian was stout and slow, it was determined that the Tianjin team would definitely lose. Unexpectedly, after the serve, Little Zheng panicked and made mistakes. Many serves went out of bounds, and many volleys were self-destructive. In the first set, Erlong Qian won 6-0 without any effort. Although he struggled in the second set, Erlong Qian's backhand volleys were calm and unhurried. Little Zheng was eager to succeed, and made more and more self-destructive balls. He only won one game in the third game, and then failed repeatedly. He finally lost again 6-2. In the third set, he tried hard to counterattack, but made no progress, and finally lost 6-2. As a result, Tianjin won 3-0. The audience criticized that in terms of individual skills, Little Zheng definitely defeated Erlong Qian, but he failed because he was young and impetuous and could not calmly face the enemy.

Educational News

Ministry of Education Explains 195

Regulations for Entrance Examinations for Vocational Schools and Middle Schools

The Ministry of Education recently issued two official orders explaining the regulations, which are excerpted below: (1) According to the Sichuan Provincial Department of Education, Article 53 of the regulations for vocational schools states that students' usual grades are calculated by combining daily homework grades and temporary test grades, with daily inspection grades accounting for two-thirds of the usual grade and temporary test grades accounting for one-third. It seems that the usual grade already includes the practical training grade. Article 58 states that those who fail in academic studies, practical training, conduct, and physical education shall not be promoted or graduate. Is it necessary to calculate academic studies and practical training grades separately? Also, does the provision of the regulations for academic study grades refer to the total grade of each subject that must be above 60 points, or must each subject pass before being promoted or graduated? I hereby request instructions, etc. The Ministry of Education explained that the student's usual grade in the regulations for vocational schools naturally includes the practical training grade. However, in order to emphasize practical training, the practical training grade should be taken out for examination to see if it is passing. As for the academic study grade, it refers to the total grade of each subject. However, those who fail in major subjects shall not be promoted or graduated. How to examine students' conduct grades and how to calculate academic study grades should be formulated by the department in accordance with Article 60 of the regulations for vocational schools and submitted for approval separately, etc. (2) According to the Social Affairs Bureau of Beiping City, Article 10 of the regulations for middle school students' graduation entrance examination states that the grades of each subject in the graduation entrance examination must be passing. Does this refer only to the grade of the entrance examination paper, or to the grade after calculation in accordance with Article 7? Also, should certificates for applying for higher education be issued for junior high school students? The Ministry of Education explained that the phrase "the grades of each subject must be passing" in Article 10 of the entrance examination regulations refers to the grade after calculation in accordance with Article 7. If the bureau is unable to issue junior high school graduation certificates, it should issue certificates for applying for higher education, etc.

Broadcasting Speech by the Municipal Education Bureau

Director Pan Speaks on Vocational Education 197

Today at 4:30 PM at the Greater China Radio Station

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau is scheduled to hold a broadcasting speech at the Greater China Wireless Radio Station on Nanjing Road at 4:30 PM today (4th). The speech will be given by Director Pan Gongzhan, and the topic will be vocational education.

Declaration of the Jinda Vocational Movement League 198

The Zhenru National Jinan University Graduate Students Vocational Movement League was established the day before yesterday. Yesterday, the league issued a declaration to respond to the two major leagues of the Pingjing Vocational Movement and decided to visit the party and government and school authorities today to petition. The declaration of the league is excerpted below: The unemployment problem has become the most serious problem in various countries around the world. However, in the past, most of the unemployed were from the labor sector. Today, even intellectuals who have received higher education feel the pain of unemployment. In this regard, the organization of the Peiping University Graduates Vocational Movement League and the subsequent response from Nanjing Central University. Comrades, in view of the fact that graduation is unemployment and that what they have learned is useless, also have the same pain. Therefore, a vocational movement league is specially organized to seek a solution to the occupation and to seek a living, and to respond to the organization of Pingjing to arouse the attention of the whole country. I humbly believe that there are very few staff in the government agencies of our country. According to the law, those who seek employment rely on individual activities, so that relatives and private individuals are mixed in, and the road to success is blocked. As for the quality of their knowledge and the diligence of their work, they are not counted. This is the first point that the government authorities should pay attention to. Today's university education has no definite standards, only knows to enroll students and teach classes. Whether the courses taught are suitable for social needs and how students should be arranged after graduation have never been asked. As a result, what is learned is useless and graduation is unemployment. This is the second point that the education authorities should pay attention to. Comrades, in view of the voice that graduation from university is unemployment, shocking the whole country, we hereby respectfully inform the government and education authorities to pay close attention and immediately seek relief measures, and we deeply hope that the entire press will give sincere sympathy. This is what we deeply hope for.

Coloring

Engineer Wu Shiming Returns to China 200

Wu Jun Shiming, from Xiuning, Anhui, holds a Bachelor of Science in Chemistry from Soochow University. He served as a teaching assistant in chemistry at Northeastern University for two years. After 918, he went to Germany to study and entered the Saxon State University of Technology in Germany to study coloring and dyeing. This spring, he obtained a coloring and dyeing engineer from the university with his thesis on blue-ground printed red flowers.

Mr. Wu Shiming

The brilliant parts of the paper will be published by the famous German Milan Textile Magazine. In addition to studying at the university, Mr. Wu also used his holidays to intern in major factories, successively interning in dyeing and printing, as well as leather making and dyeing, in the Bayer and other factories of the Dade Paint Combination. He also studied the application of various machines in the Color Soft Factory, and gained a lot of experience. It is heard that Mr. Wu will return to Shanghai by the Italian mail on the 4th, and he will surely be able to make use of what he has learned and make many contributions to the industrial world in the future.
