Shen Bao Radio Weekly

A Simple Explanation of Class A, B, and C Amplifiers 201

— Ming Xiang

In wireless machinery, the vacuum tube's primary task is amplification. In recent years, wireless technology has advanced rapidly, and although all use vacuum tubes as amplifiers, their working conditions can vary. Hence, the distinction between Class A, B, and C, each with its unique advantages. Except for a few specially designed for a particular class of amplification, most general-purpose vacuum tubes can be made into a specific class of amplifier. This requires adjusting the grid's negative potential and the input signal voltage appropriately to meet certain conditions. The principles and comparative advantages and disadvantages of these three classes of amplifiers are outlined below.

1. Class A Amplifier: When a vacuum tube is used as a Class A amplifier, the waveform of the plate output is identical to the waveform of the input signal received by the grid. Therefore, there is no distortion, which is highly desirable. Refer to Figure A, which shows the plate current/grid voltage characteristic curve of a vacuum tube. If used as a Class A amplifier, the straight-line portion between points 'a' and 'b' must be utilized. The grid potential is adjusted to approximately the midpoint of this straight line, as indicated by the dashed line. When the grid is stimulated by a signal voltage, the highest point of the positive half-cycle should not exceed zero potential, causing the grid to receive a positive charge. The highest point of the negative half-cycle should not cause the plate current to decrease excessively and reach the lower knee point 'b'. Otherwise, distortion is still difficult to avoid. Close examination of Figure A reveals that the plate current of a Class A amplifier remains constant regardless of variations in the strength of the input voltage. That is, even without any signal voltage input, the vacuum tube constantly consumes maximum power. Therefore, poor efficiency is a significant drawback of Class A amplifiers.

2. Class B Amplifier: To improve the poor efficiency of Class A amplifiers, Class B amplifiers were developed. The difference lies in employing a higher grid negative potential so that the vacuum tube's plate current is zero when no signal voltage is input, thus not consuming power. When a signal voltage is input, the vacuum tube generates plate current during the positive half-cycle, rising and falling according to the signal voltage's amplitude. During the negative half-cycle, the plate current is completely cut off, so only half of the input voltage is amplified; the other half is cut off, as shown in Figure B. If this Class B amplifier is used for audio frequency amplification, it will inevitably result in complete distortion. However, there are ways to remedy this. Usually, Class B amplifiers use two identical vacuum tubes in a push-pull connection, with each vacuum tube handling the amplification of one half-cycle. These are then combined so that the output voltage state is still consistent with the input. Refer to Figure D for a clearer understanding. Although Class B amplifiers have better efficiency, they have more components and a complex structure. Unless there is a solid understanding of the characteristics of vacuum tubes, success is often difficult to achieve.

3. Class C Amplifier: The grid's negative potential in a Class C amplifier must be higher than that of a Class B amplifier, typically about twice the voltage required to completely cut off the plate current. The voltage stimulating the grid must also be very high, with the highest point of the positive half-cycle sufficient to saturate the vacuum tube's plate current. Referring to Figure C, it is evident that the output voltage state is completely distorted. Therefore, Class C amplifiers absolutely cannot be used for audio frequency amplification. However, they are highly suitable for use as high-frequency amplifiers in broadcasting transmitters. This is because the only requirement for the output high-frequency voltage is that its envelope does not lose the original state of the input. How each voltage is distorted is effectively irrelevant. Another feature of Class C amplifiers is that their output power is always proportional to the power input to their plate.

Self-Made Intermediate Frequency Transformer Method 202

— Yingfu

In superheterodyne receiver circuits, the intermediate frequency (IF) transformer is undeniably a crucial component. However, these transformers are currently difficult to find on the market, and even when available, they are often prohibitively expensive. This puts them out of reach for budget-conscious amateur enthusiasts, leaving them sighing at the prospect of heterodyne receivers. However, these transformers can be readily made.

If the circuit includes a high-frequency transformer (commonly known as the primary and secondary coils, which, when combined, can induce the high-frequency current from the primary into the secondary coil through electromagnetic or capacitive coupling, similar to a transformer's action, hence the name high-frequency transformer, commonly used in heterodyne circuits) and two IF transformers, purchase four honeycomb coils (small) with 800 turns each and two identical coils with 400 turns each. If three IF transformers are required, add one each of the 800-turn and 400-turn coils. There are limitations on the diameter of these small coils, and the wire used is very fine, but they are generally available on the market.

First, use two of the 800-turn coils to create the high-frequency transformer. Then, use two more coils (one 800-turn and one 400-turn) to make the IF transformers, with the 400-turn coil as the primary and the 800-turn coil as the secondary.

Regardless of the number of turns, the inner diameter of all the coils is the same, so they can be strung together on a bakelite shaft as shown in the diagram. To prevent them from moving, use small pieces of cardboard to pad them or glue them in place. Drill a hole in one end of the wooden shaft to prepare for fixing them to the bakelite base with screws.

The two coils of the high-frequency transformer should be one centimeter apart, while the distance between the two coils of the IF transformer can be reduced to half a centimeter. The primary coil should be below the secondary coil, as shown in the diagram.

After the coils are fixed to the bakelite base, mount a 0.0005 microfarad capacitor directly above the secondary coil. Solder the two terminals of the capacitor to the terminals of the secondary coil, respectively.

As for the primary coil, one end can be directly connected to the plate of the associated vacuum tube, and the other end can be connected to the positive pole of the high voltage (45, 90, or 125 volts).

Do not forget that in superheterodyne circuits, the primary coil of the high-frequency transformer is accompanied by a capacitor between 0.00025 and 0.0005 microfarads. However, this capacitor is not needed in Hartley oscillator circuits.

The distance between these transformers should be at least twelve centimeters (from one central axis to another). If the IF transformers are too close, induction may occur, resulting in an unbearable squealing sound from the loudspeaker.

Using Light Bulbs as Resistors 203

— Yong Yan

Ordinary light bulbs can be used as resistors. The advantages are that they can handle relatively large currents and are inexpensive. The disadvantages are that they take up too much space and are inconvenient to install. However, there is also a major drawback: their resistance value is not fixed and varies greatly depending on the current flowing through them. If space and resistance value are not critical, light bulbs can be used as excellent and inexpensive resistors. A detailed table of the current and resistance of ordinary light bulbs is provided below for reference.

In the table, V represents volts, W represents watts, and C.h. represents candlepower. The current is measured in amperes, and the resistance is measured in ohms. The fifth column, "Resistance When Filament is Cold," is an approximate number and not precise. If the light bulb is 220 volts, its current value is approximately half that of a 115-volt bulb with the same wattage, according to the table, and its resistance value is doubled. If a light bulb's wattage and voltage are known, its current under the specified voltage can be calculated. Divide the wattage by the voltage to obtain the current. Divide the voltage by the current to obtain the resistance.

Key Points for Selecting an AC Radio 204

— Jiang Zhiban

In recent years, the wireless broadcasting industry has developed extraordinarily. Most people purchase radios for entertainment purposes. In the Jiangsu and Zhejiang areas, almost all have AC power sources, so AC radios are becoming increasingly popular because of their ease of use and lower running costs. The AC radios sold on the market are almost all dominated by imported products. These radios have at least four tubes and up to twelve tubes, and all are beautifully decorated, with excellent selectivity and sensitivity, and loud and pleasant sound. However, in recent months, manufacturers have been competing fiercely in the market, reducing prices to increase sales. However, it is difficult to have both low price and high quality. Moreover, when manufactured in large quantities, shortcuts are inevitably taken, and inspection is not always precise. As a result of this sloppy approach, the radios are not only ineffective but also easily damaged. Ordinary people, greedy for temporary bargains, often suffer considerable losses. They do not know the contents of these radios or the key points for selecting them. Based on my experience, from the standpoint of economy and high efficiency, I dare to describe them in detail for the readers.

(1) Purpose of Radio Reception: Before purchasing a radio, you should first consider the purpose of radio reception. Is the purchased radio specifically for receiving broadcasts from this city or nearby, or is it for long-distance radio reception? Is it for personal or family entertainment, or is it for use in a large venue? Generally, people use the number of tubes as the standard for selection. However, a large number of tubes does not necessarily mean that it can receive distant broadcasts or produce loud sound. It depends on the quality of the manufacturer's design and the refinement of the construction. At the same time, we must also be aware of the current broadcasting situation in China. Except for Shanghai, where there are a mix of many small and medium-powered radio stations, and the large radio station of the Central Party Department in Nanjing, there are very few radio stations scattered throughout the country, with the largest power being only one kilowatt, and the distance is always more than a thousand miles away. If you prepare a machine that can receive broadcasts from all over the country, the cost may be beyond the means of a middle-class family. Moreover, except in special circumstances, the programs of distant radio stations are unlikely to arouse interest for entertainment purposes. Therefore, from an economic point of view, the purpose of a radio for family or personal entertainment should only be to receive local or nearby large radio stations satisfactorily. In the case of Shanghai's broadcasting situation, it is essential to be able to separate them clearly. A five-tube radio with a superheterodyne circuit seems suitable for meeting these conditions (most four-tube radios on the market are not good). For radio reception in the inland, where the distance to large radio stations is farther, a seven-tube radio can be used. As for the machines suitable for other radio reception conditions, readers can deduce them.

(2) Verification of Power Supply: This is the most important point to pay attention to when selecting imported AC radios. Most of the imported products are from the United States. Therefore, its design is also based on American standards, with the power transformer input line being 110 volts and 60 cycles. In most parts of our country, the AC power supply is 220 volts and 50 cycles (the French Concession in this city is 110 volts and 50 cycles). When selecting, be sure to pay attention to the voltage and frequency of the power supply to be used and compare it with the purchased equipment to ensure that they are completely the same. Also, check that the power transformer inside American radios has not been removed and forcibly converted to 220 volts. Because the frequency is different, it is also different for the design. This kind of forcibly modified power transformer is prone to heating. Overheating will cause it to break down. Ordinary people only ask whether the voltage matches and ignore the frequency check. It must be known that a well-designed transformer will never generate excessive heat. Purchasers, rather than resting for several minutes every hour of use, sacrificing some excellent programs, and inevitably damaging the machine frequently, should be more careful when selecting, pay a slightly higher price, and get a durable radio? (To be continued)

Collecting Radio Waste Parts 205

— Xun

Often, economic constraints are enough to dampen our interest in studying radio. Especially in China, which relies exclusively on imported goods, even the simplest materials must be purchased. However, if we can carefully examine, radio materials are everywhere. The following is an introduction to waste materials that can be utilized when manufacturing small-scale radios.

(1) Steel Refined Pots: Made of aluminum, soft, and easy to shape. Never rusts. And conductivity is close to copper. This type of waste pot can be used to make capacitors, metal shields, and aluminum electrodes for Electrolyte Rectifiers.

(2) Camera Film Cases and Toothpaste Tubes: Softer in quality, suitable for making fixed capacitors or fixed plates for variable capacitors.

(3) Cigarette Tin Foil: Easiest to find. Soft and easily torn, only suitable for making large-capacity fixed capacitors. Take it because it's thin.

(4) Toothpaste and Paint Bottle Caps: Used to make mineral cups and temporary screw caps (drill a hole first, then screw on the male screw).

(5) Thermos Bottles: The metal cup and metal cover on the upper part of the bottle shell are usually made of aluminum or nickel-plated copper. The former has the same properties and uses as (1). The latter is bright and strong, has good conductivity and does not rust, and can be used as a support frame for fixed ore or grid leaks. Spring sheet wiring post. Branch nail or rotating key for variable resistor. Lamp socket spring. Vacuum tube cap clip. And wiring return pieces, etc.

(6) Thin Iron Seal Film for Paper Cigarette Cans: The surface is coated with zinc and is elastic. Suitable for replacing the thin iron film on the earpiece.

(7) Transformer, Earpiece Loudspeaker's Thin Copper Wire: Rewound on a foreign thread wooden shaft, it can be used as a low-frequency choke coil.

(8) German silver wire on electric heaters can be used as a small ohm variable resistance Ebonite.

(9) Waste Round Dry Batteries: Connect the wire to the negative electrode and bury it in the mud or throw it into the bottom of the well to replace the ground wire. The positive screw removed can be used as a wiring post.

(10) Records: Made of hard rubber Ebonite. Can be used as the panel opening of the radio and other insulation boards (such as wire pipes, etc. When drilling holes, you can use a hot knife and scissors to cut it, and bend it in boiling water).

The Most Convenient Pointer Dial 206

— Li Yuanqing

Old-fashioned pointer dials (Dials) are generally divided into one hundred grids, which have no meaning when used, only giving you an indication. The pointer dials of new radios are engraved with Kilo frequency numbers on the outside. In addition to giving you an indication when using them, they also let you know the frequency number of the radio station. This is of course much more convenient.

In fact, what we urgently want to know when receiving wireless broadcasts is not the frequency number or wavelength of the radio station, but the location and name of the radio station. In the past, when there were not many broadcasting stations, we could barely remember the names of each radio station after looking at the numbers on the pointer dial. Now, broadcasting stations are springing up everywhere. If you want to memorize them one by one, it is really too much trouble.

In order to improve the convenience of users, there is a design for a dial that indicates the name of the radio station. As shown in Figure P is a piece of black thick paper pasted on the back of the pointer dial, and L is a white chalk line drawn on the plastic board. After receiving the broadcast from a radio station, write its name on black paper in chalk. (It is best to draw a short line to match L.) When using, just pay attention to the position indicated by the white chalk line L, and you will know the name of the radio station being received. As shown in the figure, when the dial is at 35 degrees, it is the Shanghai Li Shude Hall Broadcasting Station.

Adjustment of Headphones 207

— Xun

The volume of one of my headphones increased because the bottom screw was not tightened. This is because Coulomb's law (Coulomb's law) states that the magnetic force is inversely proportional to the square of the distance, that is, after the screw is loosened, the distance between the magnet and the iron film is reduced, and the attractive force between them is several times greater. That is, the volume is also large. If you think your headphones have low and weak sound, you can fill a piece of rubber of considerable thickness at the bottom of the magnet. You can try this whether it is new or old.

If your headphones have weak volume and suffer from distortion, the above method will not work. The diaphragm is too tight against the magnet and has reached its limit. Its amplitude is blocked and restricted by the magnet. And friction causes unpleasant and weak sounds. The adjustment method is to place a thick paper circle tightly against the inner wall of the earphone. Its height can be arbitrarily stretched to find the most appropriate distance between the diaphragm and the magnet. The tone and volume can be improved.

(The author also repaired a headphone with the second method, and the result was amazing)

Spring and Autumn

Memories of Enjoying the Cool 210

— Rong Yu

The heat wave raged all day, and it wasn't until evening that I felt a little cooler; so I took a rattan chair and sat in the shade of the trees watching the children playing on the lawn, and couldn't help but recall my own childhood:

My childhood was like that of the children today; but the social situation was very different from today. All the sisters in the neighborhood were either reading "Women's Classic of Filial Piety" and "Women's Training" at home; or embroidering and needlework in high-rise buildings. In the evening, they also came to the lawn to enjoy the cool, telling stories of gods and monsters; singing popular folk songs. We boys also wanted to get in on the fun, but don't look at them being only around ten years old, the prevention of men and women was very strict, and they always chased us out; a few sharp-tongued girls even sang such a song to drive us away. "Boys are noisy; girls are noisy. Radishes don't match vegetables; turtles don't match robbers." After hearing this song, we had to walk away resentfully.

Ultimately, we couldn't stand them and thought of a way to retaliate. So, on a dark and starry night, while they were telling a story with relish, the most mischievous of us boys put on his father's black gown, painted black ink on his face, jumped up and down, and made a hissing sound in his mouth, rushing towards them. It was really effective! They were all so scared that they ran home, some shouting for help; some crying loudly. We got satisfactory revenge, and everyone clapped and cheered; and agreed not to reveal the news, lest our family members condemn us.

Girls are really easily frightened. The next day, after inquiring, these girls were all sick, and some families were busy inviting doctors; some were extending witch doctors to perform rituals, all saying that ghosts and monsters had appeared on the lawn and wanted to capture the souls of children. From then on, the lawn was quiet every night, and their traces were not seen; even we boys were locked at home by our parents and not allowed to go out.

The Story of a Watermelon 211

— Yang Yusheng

It’s hot! I can’t bear to say any more about "hot topics." Fortunately, watermelons can still bring some coolness, and the watermelon itself has a story that can be written down for everyone to enjoy.

This was told to me by my late grandfather, who had experienced the upheaval of the Jiawu Year, on a summer night twenty years ago when he was cooling off. Calling it a "story" is truly the most accurate description.

The content of this story is very simple, and it happened so many years ago, but it can still stir up feelings of regret in my heart even after twenty years. At the very least, I have been influenced by it!

Person A and Person B were casual neighbors "before the chaos." Because of the disparity in wealth, Person A often bullied Person B, sowing deep resentment. But when the chaos came, they became an inseparable pair of unfortunate companions. Like other refugees, they carried a portion of their belongings on their shoulders and backs, leading a life of wandering. The difference was that Person A had many silver ingots tied around his waist, while Person B laboriously dragged several watermelons!

It was summer, and the weather was very hot. The rivers and wells were clogged with corpses, and there was no water to drink! Although Person A possessed silver ingots, he had no opportunity to exchange them for water. Whether it was to take care of his own needs or to take revenge for past grudges, Person B very carefully and defensively ate the watermelons alone to quench his thirst. He was certainly aware that Person A was staring at the watermelons in a state of "not having a drop to spare," but no matter how much the latter pleaded, or even offered silver ingots to exchange for a watermelon, he showed absolutely no sign of yielding!

When Person B ate the last watermelon, Person A was unbearably thirsty and resorted to force to seize it, but he was at a disadvantage because Person A was accustomed to being pampered!

They parted ways. Before leaving, Person B generously threw Person A a piece of watermelon rind covered in urine and feces. This was like sweet rain and a precious treasure to Person A, who wiped it off roughly without hesitation and immediately swallowed it!

There are times when silver ingots are worthless! Watermelons are truly precious!

Jiangbei "Holland Water" 212

— Qingqu

This summer is so hot, exceeding one hundred degrees. Even the elderly, over eighty years old, say they have never seen anything like it. Now, although there have been several showers, the river levels have not returned to what they were before. Therefore, in the inland areas, the drinking water for residents is still filthy and unbearable. Although this concerns the water conservancy of the entire county and cannot be easily resolved, public hygiene is not something the local authorities pay attention to. I will talk about something very small and ask, who would be willing to study it? I have no name for this thing, so I will tentatively call it "Jiangbei Holland Water."

I think this kind of "Jiangbei Holland Water" is not unique to our Jiading area, because people from Jiangbei can go everywhere. Therefore, there must be peddlers of this kind everywhere! You can see them at street corners, men carrying a shoulder pole with a round tray on top. On the tray is a horizontal bar that can rotate. When they flick it with their hand, you can see what line it lands on, and you can get that item. Before, they used sugar figurines to attract people. Now, they are also good at seizing opportunities, using small gourd-shaped glass bottles, no more than three inches long. I heard that they first fill them with cold water, then add a small amount of saccharin, and then mix in various colorings. Therefore, the surface looks very pleasing to the eye. There are at least ten or more children surrounding this shoulder pole. Even elderly women and younger children from Jiangbei hold this tray and use this red and green water as a target. You! Think about it, is it hygienic or harmful for children to drink this in their stomachs? That is why I wrote about it, for people to study!

One day, a friend's son, only eight or nine years old, said that he drank a bottle of Holland Water from this Jiangbei man's tray, and that night, his stomach started to hurt. He cried out all night and has not recovered. I dare not say for sure if this is the reason, but because the weather is so dry and there has not been rain for more than a month, the rivers are dry and shallow, and the drinking water situation is already very dangerous. If the parents of children are not careful about this kind of Holland Water, oh! I am afraid that sickness enters through the mouth, all from a small glass bottle.

Simple Ways to Beat the Summer Heat 213

— An Ying

I often have to put on a little powder. To say that putting on a little powder also has to do with social circumstances may seem like a joke, but that's the reality. I think that when you enter society, you often have to put on a little powder. Perhaps this is the misery of modern urban women. But let's not get sidetracked. Let’s just say that I know that summer has arrived because I have to put on a little powder.

If you can't put on powder or can't put it on well, it's because it's summer, and sweat is being excreted from the pores of your face. This is what women find troublesome, putting on powder in the summer.

But now I don't want to say much about putting on powder in the summer, I want to talk about my ways to beat the summer heat.

My ways to beat the summer heat are really very simple:

If I have some spare money in my pocket, I go to the ice cream shop to drink a cup or two of shaved ice, or a serving or two of ice cream.

When I have too much time, I go to the Rongguang Theater after lunch and sit there until dusk. The admission ticket for Rongguang is thirty cents. The theater has air conditioning, so you can watch continuously or take a nap. Once you buy a ticket, you can sit there until you want to leave, or until eleven o'clock at night. Going to the movie theater to beat the summer heat is probably a method I invented.

If I could take a small boat to Huangpu River, I know that would also be a good way to beat the summer heat, but I am afraid of the boat capsizing and falling into the water, so I often go to the dock and stand for an hour or two. Standing on the dock to enjoy the river breeze and cool off is also a good way to beat the summer heat?

When there is really no other way, I stroll around in the small courtyard, or play the piano for some time. I am a great lover of music, and playing a sad piece of music can really help me get rid of some of the heat and sweat.

My ways to beat the summer heat are not brilliant. For me, summer is ultimately a season of misery.

The Park After the Rain 214

— Chen Liang

Dark clouds were chasing closely behind, and as soon as I stepped into the Yating Pavilion, the rain came down, thick and heavy, like thousands of arrows shooting down from mid-air, stirring up mist and spreading out, with countless small circles crowding and floating on the surface of the pond. Ashan hugged her leather dog and huddled in the corner of the pavilion, very well-behaved, her little eyes staring at each raindrop like an arrow. "Whish whish whish..." The brave and strong sound of the rain. A frog squatted on a large lotus leaf, silently, letting the rain pour down on it, pour down on it.

A gust of wind tousled Ying's hair, a gust of wind blew off my straw hat: "What an annoying wind!" However, we liked having this rainstorm. In the sky, a pile of dark clouds was pushed away by a pile of white clouds, and the rain stopped. When the white clouds dispersed, a blue color filled the sky, and the first ray of sunlight shone on the frog's back, as if it were happy. "Croak, croak, croak" it cried. The trees were revitalized and particularly energetic, just enduring the attack of the storm, and now receiving the cleansing of the sunlight, gaining a new life.

The whole garden was a lush green, with patches of red where the rain had scattered the monthly roses. Everything was awakened!

"Ying, do you love this new world?"

"But I'm also afraid of that moment of the storm!"

"Why be afraid of that little bit? It's a necessary process."

Ying led Ashan, walking by my side, talking, with a pure heart. On the carpet-like lawn, my feet sank into the water, like a sponge in a basin. Ashan threw the leather dog into a puddle, shouting, "Doggy drinks water, doggy drinks water," her innocent and ignorant appearance was enough to make people laugh.

The bar was empty, the white-clothed waiter with a pointy chin was standing there blankly, the ashtrays were dozing off on the white tablecloth, and not one of the usual high-class people could be found. Lonely, the carnations in the flower vase drooped their heads. Eaves dripping tears, sycamores dripping tears, rose vines dripping tears, the despair of the end of the century.

However, this park after the rain was awakened, filled with vitality, new life.

Hot Topics on Poetry 215

— (Yangzijiang)

The Xujiahui Observatory was established only a little over sixty years ago, but this year's heat has exceeded the record of any year in the observatory's past. Sketches from the Ice-Drinking Studio 216

— Zhu Shouchang

The large blades of the electric fan spin wildly, and the waiters in plain clothes bustle back and forth like bees. Coca-Cola, Coca-Cola, the eye-catching billboards shine brightly. The descriptive words for cocoa, vanilla, orange, mango, and ice cream, and the names for lemon, red bean, fruit syrup, grape juice, and shaved ice are spat out at the mouth and written on paper. A wheat straw is held in cherry lips and sucked on, and soda bubbles dance in tall glass cups. The doorboy has not a moment of leisure, batches of guests leave, and pairs of lovers enter to welcome the new.

X X X X

"Ice" is large, written on a wooden sign: large cup one hundred and twenty, medium cup eighty, small cup..., and there is also an oval wooden barrel painted red with "Beijing (or Tianjin) Sour Plum Soup," with the price list listed in the same way. Several ordinary tables are covered with white cloth, and the different cups are neatly inverted on the basins, forming a natural pattern. Drinkers in long gowns and customers in short clothes often feel the narrowness of the seats due to overcrowding.

X X X X

In the shade of the streets and roadsides, an ice cream machine is placed by the foot, and old enamel basins filled with water contain thick, tall, glass cups. The old peddler, although wearing a cloth short shirt, does not button the entire row of buttons, and a tuft of hair is lined on his purplish-black belly. Beads of sweat drip from his forehead, but his mouth shouts wildly: "Top-notch, only ten cents!" Laborers, coolies, and street children surround his stall, with happy smiles floating on their faces, slowly enjoying the cheap ice cream.

Where the Travel Led

Qingdao in Summer 217

— Nangongsheng

During these dog days of summer, when the scorching sun is oppressive and the heat reaches over one hundred degrees, everyone wants to find a summer resort to pass the sweltering weather. Although Mogan Mountain and Lushan are cool, because they are high in the mountains, the enjoyment of all material comforts is relatively inconvenient, so it is far better to go to Qingdao for summering, which is more convenient and suitable.

Qingdao is a peninsula along the coast, surrounded by sea on three sides and land on one side. All year round, it is warmed by the sea breeze, which regulates the climate, so in summer it becomes an excellent summer resort.

Since Qingdao was leased to and operated by Germany, after the changes of the European War, it was recovered from the hands of Japan and placed under the political control of our country. During these twenty years of experience, all the construction has gradually become complete. Especially because Qingdao is a summer resort area, the facilities for summering are becoming more and more perfect. There is Huiquan Bathing Beach, Huiquan Hotel and Qingdao Hotel along the coast, the first to fifth parks, wide sandy beaches, the Qingdao Cafe for dancing, and everything else, all of which are enough for summerers to enjoy supreme comfort and coolness.

In the summer, the several hotels along the coast of Qingdao are filled with tourists who come to escape the summer heat. In the evening, strolling on the sandy beach by the sea, enjoying the sea breeze, is such a happy and refreshing experience. Huiquan Bathing Beach can be considered one of the best bathing beaches in the country. There is a bathing beach that can accommodate thousands of bathers, a sandy beach that stretches for several miles, and fully complete facilities. In the summer, when the sun sets, you can see thousands of bathers in the sea undergoing baptism. Men, women, old, young, pretty, ugly, Europeans, Americans, Japanese, Indians, Chinese, it can be said to be an international human race exhibition, all wearing beautiful and white bathing suits, rippling in the sea, sitting and lying on the sandy beach, as if there were no summer in the world.

The vastness of the First Park can be said to be beyond people's expectations, with a site of more than a thousand acres, containing mountains and plains. The park has ancient trees that can be embraced, thousands of cherry blossoms, neat short cypresses, winding mountain paths, and flat sandy roads. In this sleepy season, it is common to see many cars traveling through the park, winding up the mountain road, covered by the shade of the trees, and truly not knowing that there is a summer with temperatures over one hundred degrees. Therefore, people who escape the summer heat in Qingdao cannot help but be happy and forget to return.

The temperature in Qingdao in summer, at noon, is at most eighty degrees, but in the evening it is between sixty and seventy degrees. It does not have the low temperatures of Mogan Mountain and Lushan, nor the high heat of Beiping and Hankou. It is exactly a suitable place to escape the summer heat. It is only when you see the Japanese shops on Liaocheng Road, the towering Japanese Loyal Soul Monument, and the Japanese Shrine where Japanese people pay their respects, that you can think of the ambitions of schemers for Qingdao. People who come to escape the summer heat should not only know that Qingdao is a good place to escape the summer heat, but also forget the danger of Qingdao. I am afraid that in a few years, you will not be allowed to come to Qingdao to escape the summer heat, and it will become the second of the four northeastern provinces.

Watching Dancing at a Shanghai Dance Hall to Beat the Summer Heat 218

— Jiamenglulu

Dancing wildly all night, in unison, singing and laughter filling the four walls, glibly calling it civilization from the West, happily watching the pavilions near the Autumn River, changing colors, expressions illusory, changing steps, shifting shapes, poses charming, Europe and Asia together truly comparable, how do they tease each other and enjoy themselves.

Ancestral robes exposed before my eyes, the fragrance of beautiful women brushed against the banquet, soaking in the beauty of Miao women, one-third charming, faintly barbaric customs, the second month of the year, seeing this good man on this very evening, and the lady in green as well, meeting to discuss state affairs, talents like this, giving their best years to instruments and strings.

Financial Silver Prices Rise Repeatedly

Spot Gold Drops Another 3.4 Yuan 219

American Silver Certificates Show Weakness on the Market

Buying Activities Result in Continued Stability

The gold market is under pressure from silver prices, and sentiment is weak. Spot prices have fallen steadily, but volume has increased sharply, and selling pressure is relatively weak, making rebounds inevitable. Although the market suffered a sharp drop yesterday due to rumors about American silver certificates, the result was still relatively stable. Early in the morning, due to the continued rise in overseas silver markets, the forward silver price on the Metal Exchange rose by 0.3 to 0.47 percent. The price of spot gold in London rose by one penny, exchange rates lengthened slightly, American cotton contracted by three pounds, and American wheat and stocks both fluctuated. With silver prices only rising and not falling, it is difficult to boost market sentiment. Off-exchange trading immediately fell to 75.6 yuan. After 5 yuan was broken, market sentiment became even weaker, with supply exceeding demand. Although the market was stable after opening, Reuters suddenly reported that US Senator Thomas's request to promptly issue new silver currency had been answered by the Treasury Department. The Treasury Secretary stated that the issuance of silver certificates would be brought forward as much as possible, with 1,204,000 "one-dollar" silver certificates and 11,640,000 "five-dollar" certificates about to be printed. "Ten-dollar" certificates will be issued next week or the week after, "twenty-dollar" certificates are scheduled for early September, and "one-hundred-dollar" certificates are scheduled for mid-October, all of which will be issued successively. It was also said that silver would be purchased continuously and issued permanently, causing great uncertainty and triggering a price decline. The foreign exchange market also loosened accordingly, with a rapid downward trend. However, because the gold market had been falling for many days in a row, volume had increased significantly, and selling pressure was relatively weak. After a general influx of buying from big players at low prices, there were also rumors that the central bank had intervened in cash. The price rose again after falling, and gradually pulled up. Bank appetites were strong, and after that, Chinese merchants also developed an appetite for buying, and Cantonese merchants even came to cover their short positions. Both the foreign exchange and gold markets became tight. Although there was some fluctuation in between, buying sentiment recovered, and the market was particularly firm at noon. In the afternoon, bank appetite remained strong, and the market was particularly firm, but sentiment appeared slightly uncertain. Sources of supply frequently appeared at high prices. Rumors from Bombay reported a slight deterioration. General sellers were unwilling to give in, and gold prices fell once again, but Cantonese merchants continued to buy, and there was still residual buying power, and the price was pulled up again. Saigon Rice Opens for Sale at 11 Yuan for the First Time

Small Jiao Surpasses Large Triangle and Ke Xian Surpasses 1 Jiao

Yesterday, after the rise of Small Jiao, it was snatched up by the inland, and the price also rose by 1 jiao. The whole city bought 4,000 bags of Small Jiao from this street, and the inland bought more than 7,000 bags of machine-milled Ke Xian rice. It is heard that after our country's drought, the production price has gradually increased. Yesterday, the same product was quoted at 4 yuan, 3 jiao, 8 fen, which has increased by 2 jiao, 6 fen. Therefore, people's hearts are unanimously upward. A hundred bags of No. 1 Saigon, which arrived in Shanghai a few days ago, were opened for trial on the market, and the price was 11 yuan. This price can make a profit according to the cost, but this price of 11 yuan has been magnified by 3 or 4 jiao in the market, because the importers also purchased a batch of Annam sugar (price 11 yuan, 7 jiao) and used this to compete with Saigon, so they are willing to let go of the price. If the next batch of confirmed orders arrive, or the previous arrivals are sold at a discounted price, then the 11 yuan Saigon may not be able to stand firm.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Some Words on Mr. Cao's Proposal of "A Few Small Problems of the People's Language" 241

— A Long

Yesterday, Mr. Cao Juren raised a few small problems regarding the people's language in the Free Talk section, inviting former colleagues of the National Language Research Society and gentlemen concerned about language issues to discuss them. After reading this letter, I cannot help but chatter again.

I must declare first that I am not a colleague of the National Language Research Society, nor am I one concerned about language issues. I am one who is scolded as having feudal thoughts, but I am ultimately a member of the masses, and I will speak a few words in the capacity of the masses.

Many articles on the people's language have been published in the supplement, but they are mostly empty talk, lacking practical solutions for the people's language. Therefore, we no longer see the editor publishing such articles. Now, seeing Mr. Cao raise a few small problems about the people's language, I cannot help but be eager to try, like Feng Fu encountering a tiger.

In Mr. Cao's letter, what I agree with most are the two sentences: "The issue of the people's language is all about the clamor of gongs and drums, but no official appears on the stage." Indeed, having advocated for the masses, please let a few writers who advocate for the people's language first create a few standard texts in the people's language, so that everyone can read and admire them. Relying solely on ideals in the mind and using the attitude of a village woman scolding in the streets is useless. The result is only showing off and considering it a successful event, achieving the goal. What contribution does this make to the masses? What real benefits are there?

Now, I will not discuss the five small problems raised by Mr. Cao. In addition to the five small problems raised by Mr. Cao, I will first raise an even smaller problem, which is that I do not understand the recently loudly advocated people's language at all. What exactly are people advocating for now, the people's language or the people's writing, or writing within it, or advocating the people's writing while the language is also within it?

Therefore, the first question I raise is, should the people's language and the people's writing be discussed together, or should they be discussed separately?

If we talk about the people's writing, I have one opinion first. The so-called people's writing must naturally consider the lower classes of society in order to be called the people's writing and to enable the masses of the lower classes to speak, understand, and write. However, alas, most of the masses in our country are illiterate, friends who do not recognize a single character. The literate population in our country is only a little over ten percent, while the illiterate population is more than eighty percent. (Please forgive me for not having accurate statistics here, but I heard others say so.) And the so-called little over ten percent are the intellectual minority among the masses. If we talk about the people's writing in this situation, the result will still be a few intellectuals playing with words, showing off their skills, while the so-called masses are still being deceived. Therefore, to use the people's writing, the fundamental problem lies in popularizing education first. If education is not popularized, no matter what you advocate, the so-called masses will still be as bewildered as Grandma Liu entering the Grand View Garden for the first time.

If we talk about the people's language, naturally there will be a few experts in the study of the national language who will talk about it in a coherent and authentic manner, and it is not necessary for me, an outsider, to say too much. However, from my feudal-minded perspective, the method of adopting the people's language cannot succeed by picking a sentence here and a sentence there. It must also designate a local dialect as the standard. Assuming that the Beijing dialect is taken as the standard, because the Beijing dialect is the most common, if we can do our best to promote and implement it, no matter how "official" the language may be, over time, we will naturally achieve the result of being able to speak, hear, and write it. If we say that because it is the people's language, we go to the masses to find it, it is like building a house and asking passersby for advice, which will not be completed in three years, and we will never find any reason.

The above is the argument for discussing the people's language and the people's writing separately. If we say that the people's language requires the ability to write, speak, and hear, then the ability to speak must mean the ability to write, and the ability to write must mean the ability to hear. It seems unnecessary to discuss them separately, but writing and language are still somewhat different. One is used with the mouth and ears, and the other is used with the hands and eyes. According to the current situation, there is still a need to discuss them separately. Therefore, my opinion is:

First, it is necessary to popularize education, so that the masses can first learn several hundred to a thousand characters, so that there is a way to start.

Second, it is necessary to first designate a local dialect as the standard, which is easier to start. The dialect cannot be found from the lower classes of society.

These are the author's opinions. What do the readers think?

Little Thief 242

— Cun Yin

The newspaper publishes a piece of news:

...Wang Genlin, fourteen years old. While stealing coal dust loaded on a truck, he was accidentally crushed to death by the wheels.

Around the thatched cottage by the small bridge, everyone knows about this little guy, Genlin. And everyone will tell you a story; a sad one.

His father was sent to prison when he was eight years old. For failing to repay the landlord's debt.

His mother died two years ago, exactly.

This child is all alone, with only an old grandmother who is deaf and blind, and relies on her grandson every day to live.

This lively Genlin has a heart that is filial to his grandmother.

A short, short six years, basically unnoticed.

Relying on his own hands, he goes to the factory every day to earn some money. Living like this, he would never curse his fate. Genlin thought in his heart:

How smoothly I am doing. I have not the slightest dissatisfaction with my ancestral fields.

He often stares at the sky in a daze. Sometimes, he would even shed tears when he thought of his parents. However, in an instant, his sorrow would be blown away by the wind in space.

Little Genlin has a quick mind.

People in the factory are very fond of him. Some workers would share half of their flatbread with him.

Naturally, he would often think of the people who shared the flatbread with him. When he finished his own work, he also liked to help others finish their work. Some people said:

"He is so affectionate, this little guy."

Alas! The factory siren has not sounded for more than two months. The two large iron gates are tightly closed. A white sign with black characters is also hung on the gate.

Genlin heard from others that the factory was closed. He was anxious. Anxious...

There is no way. My grandmother needs to be fed. I have to live too!

So, he stole three cakes from the flatbread shop. This is the first time!

I don't like this next time. Alas! How fast my heart is beating!

Tomorrow, my stomach will be hungry again! Blame this useless stomach!

"Genlin, you have to find some other work!..."

Grandma has really been hungry for a long time.

"Grandma, I'll go find something to eat!..."

Walking slowly on the street. A pair of dull eyes constantly dart around at every shop on the street.

Suddenly, he saw a crowd of people over there. Curious, he also rushed over to see!

Stealing!

"He stole our things! Not just this time!"

The shop assistant of the flour shop, holding a wooden stick, said to the people surrounding him. That Shandong accent is so terrible!

"Beat him! Warn him!"

"Thief who steals things! Beat him to death."

"Beat him! Beat him hard!"

The people watching the excitement were all shouting.

Genlin squeezed into the crowd. Secretly poked his head out to take a look at what the thief was like.

Oh! That person who once shared flatbread with him.

He saw that person holding his head in a panic, walking away from the crowd. Oh, he also has a wife and children!

I pray for him, that the beating doesn't hurt!

Genlin only had this wish. He felt even colder about the reward for stealing things!

A fragile heart!

Genlin was listlessly wandering on the road.

Occasionally, he discovered a truck loaded with a lot of coal dust. What a good opportunity!

Climbing up from the wheels. Desperately stuffing the coal dust into the bag.

Unintentionally, the car started moving.

Panicked, he jumped down. Poor little life! Crushed by the wheels! Miserable! Intestines!...Blood...

Little thief! Little thief who doesn't take the right path!

The people on the road were shouting again!

The old grandmother at home is still waiting for a time to be full.

Waving Fan, Rapid Draft 243

— Tan Shui

The term "love" can only be enjoyed by noble people, another class is called "having an affair".

It is indeed wrong to translate women as "dogs," because if they are also humans, if she is a dog, then the man should be a male dog. Therefore, it is better to translate it as "hook," because if they were not "hooks," how could they turn with amorous glances and cause trouble for thousands?

The Chinese teacher said: "Chinese is the language of our own country, so no matter what, we would rather give up other subjects and have to pay attention to Chinese." The English teacher said: "English is one of the most common languages in the world today, and it will be greatly related to 'occupation' and 'position' in the future, so students have to pay attention to English." The physical education teacher said: "Physical education is the foundation of everything. If you don't have a healthy body, what's the use of having great knowledge?" The teachers are fighting against each other like this, all they want is to do a better job of teaching their own subjects so that they can win a word of praise from the principal. However, it is the students who suffer, how can they follow? In the end, it's still just "everything is not good."

After playing in the New World for two months, I actually wrote an "impression record." Sometimes, I even mistakenly called the store name as the street name. However, after the book came out, it was actually labeled with the title of XX. Isn't it a joke?

Spring in the Height of Summer 244

Demon 245

— Zhong Shuo

Wang Xiaomazi led Xingfa forward in large strides, frighteningly, holding a ghost-head knife in his right hand and tightly grasping the hemp rope that bound Xingfa's hands behind his back with his left hand, his face full of murderous intent, like escorting a prisoner to the execution ground. However, it was not yet dark, and his gait inevitably carried a sense of panic.

"X your grandmother, won't you walk faster? I'll reward you with a knife!" Xiaomazi's right hand raised, the ghost-head knife gleamed, followed by two "ham kicks" to Xingfa.

Hanging two lines of tears, Xingfa glanced back, catching sight of Xiaomazi's hideous face, and the slow pace followed by an accelerated rate.

"Damn it, what kind of reason does the Red Spear Society have?" Xingfa cursed in his heart: "I borrowed twenty yuan from him before the second half of February, and now he wants sixty-five yuan from me, including principal and interest, less than three months, and the interest is forty-five yuan? Even 'usury' is not this much! Looking at it this way, what Lao Si said about Xiaomazi wanting my wife is true!"

Although the fire of anger was burning, he dared to be angry but dared not speak out, and only a few wrinkles appeared on his dark face. This frustration caused the pace to slow down again, so he received a few knocks on the back with the back of the knife, and the slow pace consciously accelerated again.

In the midst of such high kicks, the colorful clouds in the northwest corner gradually disappeared. Suddenly, Wang Xiaomazi stood still, looking back, seeing nothing, only the sound of dogs barking trembling, carried by the wind. Xiaomazi did not panic, and still forced Xingfa forward.

After another moment, hurried footsteps gradually approached, and when he turned around, three different voices intertwined and said in unison:

"Is that Brother Wang!"

"Exactly, is no one chasing us!"

"Who dares? Haha..." Again, intertwined voices.

"So, Tang Huzi is here too!" Xiaomazi said.

"I saw Lao Si and Chengde Ge running to the main gate, so I came to help." Tang Huzi continued to answer.

"Don't chat!" Chengde and Lao Si raised their red-tasseled spears and took the lead in striding forward.

It wasn't long after dark, and they all entered the village. After entering the house, Xingfa was tied into a ball, and Lao Si held a whip and questioned him while whipping him.

"This year, the rice in the fields is all dried up, you..."

Page 21

Realizing that this address was disrespectful "...the several masters certainly know that I will try my best to raise the twenty yuan I owe, even if I don't eat, as for the interest,..."

Xiaomazi was lying on the rattan chair waving a palm-leaf fan, and shouted loudly:

"Lao Si! Don't nag him, just ask him if he can pay the sixty-five yuan!"

Amidst the groans, Lao Si's whip was raised high again.

"I don't think you can squeeze much oil and water out of him!" The oblivious Tang Huzi said coldly.

Xiaomazi's face immediately sank, and Chengde led Tang Huzi to a secluded place, explaining that Xiaomazi had taken a fancy to Xingfa's wife. Only then did Tang Huzi realize.

"Big brother is asking if you can pay the interest? Otherwise, you can mortgage your wife! Keep crying, it's not like your grandfather died!" Lao Si's whip was about to fall with the voice.

Xingfa thought of his wife, his nose soured, and two lines of tears rolled down like beans.

In the yard, the sound of the brothers' guns and knives whistling was particularly crisp, the jumping of the black shadows under the moonlight was like the dance of barbarians, and the panting of the people outside the house mixed with the groaning inside the house rippled in the air, appearing particularly solemn.

A Gui 246

— Hai Bo

I. A Gui's Occupation

Thunderous car sounds break the silence of the city. How early! The sky is still the color of fish belly, A Gui pushes a rectangular manure cart to every street, every lane, every store, every residence, pouring the things excreted by others into his own cart barrel by barrel. Knocking on this house's door and then knocking on that house's...

Rumble, rumble...

The sound of iron wheels kissing the stone road.

Dong, dong, dong...

The sound of fists hitting the door.

This life has a history of many years with him, ask a few old ayis, everyone knows that flat face, with a beard all over his chin.

People don't treat him as a human being, and even he himself has forgotten that he is a human being. His sense of smell is like a dog's - of course not a Pekingese dog squatting next to a young lady or madam - it is the kind of dog that opens its mouth and eats the pile of yellowish-orange when it sees it. He can't smell that the excrement is smelly, he relies entirely on this thing to exchange for food.

Everyone knows that what you eat comes out as manure. People are always suspicious of dogs who exchange manure for food! Who knows? In the heavenly city, there are many dog-like people living in hell.

A Gui, with a flat face and a beard all over his chin, is one of the many dog-people.

II. A Gui's Illness

The accumulated filth of day after day, month after month, year after year, seems about to erupt, A Gui's stomach is always gurgling. His buttocks are particularly intimate with the toilet.

It must be because he lay on the street last night and caught a cold, and he has been having diarrhea more than a dozen times this morning. His intestines are knotted, and he always has so little diarrhea. His anus is burning hot, and it hurts when he wipes it with rough paper, and his limbs are weak.

Dysentery! He understands his symptoms. But he has no money, he is not qualified to see a doctor - even the doctor's toilet is emptied by him.

The next day, A Gui still pushes the manure cart out very early, supporting his illness. He has been to the back door of the doctor's house, but he knows that the doctor's clean fingers will not deign to press on his dirty wrist.

He pushes the heavy car body again without hesitation. Heavy steps, to knock on another house's door.

Back in the grass shed, he can't hold on anymore. He falls to the ground on his bunk. But his stomach is acting up again, and he gets up again to squat on the toilet.

Holding up his waistband, he falls back on the bunk, his head heavy as if he has a toilet bowl on it. His hands are pressed tightly on his stomach, and his feet are moving like bellows, moving, moving.

The sun peeks in from the window like it is visiting a patient, kissing his filthy face and filthy clothes.

Unable to bear the pain, unable to bear the heat, he uneasily rolls over to this side, and rolls over to that side.

Like a wounded dog, restless and uneasy, he rolls on the ground.

Bowing and squatting on the toilet, holding up his waistband, he comes back, once, twice, three times...

A person who makes a living by eating manure, who knows? He fell ill on it.

On the Art of Scheming 247

— Wei Nan

God has arranged people's brains to prepare you to think of ways, even the stupidest person will think in their brain, so when God created people, he handed over to people the skill of "thinking".

This thing called "thinking", in people's brains, has indeed given us many improvements in any kind of thing or matter. Therefore, people have today's progress because they have this "thinking". Because they constantly "think", "thinking" has become a combat skill today. However, everyone can "think", but there is a distinction between the wise and the inferior in "thinking". The important key lies here.

Now it is almost an era dedicated to using "thinking". Whoever can "think" and "think" surprisingly will win the victory. However, now is an era of economic terror, all industries are declining, and everything is not going well. In the city, financial tightness only leads to abnormal development, such as the increase in the number of unemployed people, the lack of growth in legitimate businesses, luxury goods fill the stores, and the propertied class only seeks their own enjoyment and momentary intoxication. Therefore, some so-called things that cater to the trend of the times emerge in response, such as cinemas, dance halls, coffee shops, and trends surge and fill the buildings next to the road. In such an acute era, a large labor force is formed, driven to the streets and alleys, spending a miserable life of wandering and unemployment. Therefore, a group of people who can "think", "think" faster than others, and "think" to suit other people's tastes, sell their skills everywhere, such as flattering, supporting the stage, being a running dog, ... In short, in front of the person they admire, they act like a woman, flaunting their charm!

If it doesn't go as planned, in other words, if you don't squeeze in, you will "think" in hundreds of ways, and even sharpen your head as much as possible to drill and operate. And the art of drilling and operating has two aspects, smooth and unsmooth. The so-called smooth aspect is that the three methods of wind, horse and bull are all in place, so when you start drilling, you must be like a loach in the mud, and you can't see the hole, so as to prevent later people from drilling in the same way. The so-called unsmooth aspect is that the person being flattered feels that you are too heavy, and the person being blown feels that you are too loud. Losing these two skills, of course, we cannot talk about "wind". If you want to drill and operate successfully, you have to implement the principle of wind, horse and bull.

Notice To Mr. Wu Ci, your letter has been received with respect. It was previously said that this journal would change the method of receiving remuneration, but it was abandoned due to the inconvenience of implementation. Please bring your articles to the accounting department with seals from the 6th to the 10th, or the 16th to the 20th of this month. This is the reply. Supplement Editorial Office

Fiction

One Night (4) 248

— Li Huaiying

Thick coal smoke poured into the room from the open window, abnormally foul. Mrs. Zheng's red eyes were immediately blinded by the flying coal smoke, and she hurriedly raised her hand to rub them. Mrs. Sun saw this clearly and shouted loudly as if she had won:

"Good, good, who told you to be sharp-tongued and criticize people, God is punishing you! Serves you right! Serves you right!"

Mrs. Liu moved her small feet and hurried to the window to close it. A few streaks of black smoke dust hung on Mrs. Xing's fair skin. She didn't notice, but she said as if she was inspired by the scene;

"It's really annoying, we have to eat coal smoke every day!"

Not far outside their window, there was a small factory with a chimney as thick as a bowl spewing out foul-smelling, black smoke dust all day and night. When the wind was favorable, it would blow into the house in gusts.

Mrs. Zheng had already rubbed her eyes, still not forgetting to smile slowly and continue:

"In a few days, you won't be able to eat it even if you want to."

Her words were protested by Mrs. Xing;

"Then haven't your eyes been blinded enough!"

No one noticed that the coal smoke dissipated in the room after turning a few times.

Outside, everything was hidden in darkness. The windows of the thirteen-story foreign apartment building nearby revealed lights of different colors, and shadows swayed in the windows, occasionally drifting with the songs of men and women singing together. A radio was also broadcasting Shanghai ditties in other houses in the alley.

What about their house? Everything was incomparable, it was desolate, it was miserable, and at the same time there was stuffiness and anger.

Because of this, it was easy to arouse their hatred; why do others have the good fortune to enjoy themselves, and they are just living a hard and difficult life, and now, it seems that they have reached the end of their lives. If they didn't resist Japan, wouldn't they still be able to live in Jilin? So, did they do something wrong?

They talked some nonsense again, but it was all of the unpleasant kind, and some people had tears flowing quietly in their eyes.

"Mrs. Sun, would you sing another section?"

Whenever they feel restless and helpless, they need Mrs. Sun to defuse the situation; because she can sing a few ditties. Mrs. Liu saw the sad tears in other people's eyes, and proposed this because she wanted to relieve the pain in people's hearts in a short time.

Supplement of Shen Bao, this port Film Special

Further Discussion on Dialect and Vernacular Films (Part 2) 249

— Danfeng

Reply to Mr. Tang Na

Everyone acknowledges that the vernacular movement of the May Fourth era accomplished unification. However, since a portion of them rebelled, and another portion surrendered to feudal forces, while the vanguard still hasn't abandoned its mission. Regarding this point, because the vernacular unification movement is quite beneficial to us, a portion rebelled for their own interests, even returning to classical Chinese in an attempt to regress to the past. On the other hand, we need to accelerate social reform through culture, so language unification is definitely not a task to be ignored. As for films and dramas that educate the masses, to increase their artistic effectiveness, we may adopt a portion of the vernacular, or a certain play may be temporarily performed in a local dialect. This is merely one of our means, and it definitely does not contradict the principle of a common language. Furthermore, we will produce copies of films needed by the masses in a certain local dialect. However, this should definitely not be interpreted the same way as the "business sense" of film merchants. Therefore, Mr. Tang Na's vigorous advocacy of Cantonese sound films, in fact, encourages this business-minded trend. Moreover, even if films are made in Cantonese, they might not be understood by the people of Shantou. It goes without saying that they would lose the national scope they should have. Furthermore, according to his argument, if dialects are allowed to develop fully, will the countryside revert to primitive times? This is what we want to ask. Originally, dialects are very primitive things. Regarding his statement of "division for unification," we have already explained it earlier. Now, we want to strengthen the leading role, to make it tend towards unification, rather than division.

He said: "At present, the language and even the social economy of the Han people are inherently divided… The unity of the nation did not begin to be divided by the promotion of dialect films, dramas, and literature." He also said: "The process of language unification is definitely not as simple as Mr. Danfeng described." As for who is dividing the Chinese nation, we have already explained that earlier. As for the latter's theory that the cultural movement is useless, that is simply unacceptable. Indeed, we acknowledge that language unification must rely on economic and political actions as the main driving force, while the cultural movement is also always one of the main driving forces. I ask, are we currently engaged in a cultural movement? Even after the entire economic foundation is reformed, will a sound cultural movement still be needed? In the current stage of China, the objective environment does not allow us to eliminate illiteracy, this is a fact, but we must move towards that path. Film is a powerful tool for educational work, why shouldn't it shoulder the task of unifying language? And the common language we are now building is intended to unify the language of the masses of the entire Han ethnicity. The theory that culture is useless is certainly absolutely wrong, and saying that culture cannot promote language unification is also a cowardly misinterpretation. From the May Fourth movement to the present, we have never abandoned the work of unification. And now, whoever can promote the unification of language and culture will achieve leadership victory.

According to his argument, if things continue to develop, because he wants to enable the masses to read, write, and speak quickly, he will propose removing Chinese characters, using Latin letters for phonetic transcription, or Practical Esperanto. As for whether the future development of language and culture will have this prospect, we dare not predict yet. However, in the current stage, if we abolish Chinese characters, which have become compatible with the living habits of the masses and become a weapon of struggle, that would be an unreasonable and arbitrary move that deviates from objective reality, if we believe that we are not impractical dreamers who are detached from reality.

Regarding this point, we can learn from the experiment of the Japanese Ministry of Education's vigorous efforts to abolish Chinese characters and replace them with "Katakana." The result is that second-year middle school students cannot understand a very short letter written in "Katakana," and similarly, if Chinese people write letters using phonetic symbols, it would not necessarily be easy to understand. However, phonetic symbols still have their use in the common language unification movement, provided that they do not inherently harm the growth of the common language. As for abolishing Chinese characters and abolishing China's inherent culture, this is in any case a high-sounding tone that is detached from the masses and non-struggling. Perhaps we can develop theoretical discussions in this direction in the future, but what we need now is to build a common and applicable language for the general public with substantial content based on Chinese characters.

Chinese films, up to now, although they cannot penetrate factories or the countryside, and neither in content nor in form can they become what the masses urgently need. But we are undoubtedly moving towards that path. At the same time, Mr. Tang Na also acknowledges that there is already a kind of Mandarin circulating among the masses, and this is the best blueprint for the subtitles of common language sound and silent films.

Not at all wrong, no one can independently create a standard common language, but it must be "done by the masses themselves." However, truly conscientious intellectuals who serve the masses, go deep into the masses to discover and select, and express it in films or other works of art, is definitely not a crime, right? Mr. Tang Na should not maliciously misinterpret this point. (End)

Film Reviews

Review of "It Happened One Night" 250

— Ling He

ItHappenedOneNight

——Grand Theater——

Similar to "Lady for a Day," Frank Capra adopted a story that has very little truth, but he used superior expressive skills, making people believe that everything he said was true, like reality in a dream. Although waking up feels infinitely empty, at the time of dreaming, one feels a certain degree of comfort or sorrow.

Indeed, the story of this film is very fanciful. If we acknowledge that the development of characters cannot be separated from economic or environmental determinism, then from the great banker, the rich daughter, to the unemployed reporter, the characters are all unrealistic and become unique in the world. At least they are all good guys in the eyes of the story author. In terms of moral concepts, he created several good people longed for by those with old ideas. The banker unconditionally dotes on his daughter, the rich daughter surprisingly falls in love with an unemployed newspaper reporter, and the unemployed newspaper reporter is even a gentlemanly sensualist. In order to pursue a woman, he twice abandoned a reward of ten thousand gold. Perhaps a sophist would explain it this way, because the newspaper reporter knew whose daughter the young lady was. Obtaining her love and further marrying her is more reliable and stable than temporarily obtaining twenty thousand gold. But on the screen, it tells us that when the young lady expressed her love to him in the small hotel, he rejected her. This gentlemanly exaggeration does not intend to play on the money or the love. On the surface, this and the young lady running to the newspaper reporter seems to be a contradiction. And this contradiction is often found in unrealistic works of art.

If it is said that after the young lady's suitcase was stolen on the long-distance bus, although she was poor, she could still run to her new husband within the possible range (she still has more than four yuan). Then, the later scenes would have no way to unfold. Of course, we don't have to ask this way, but this story is structured in many accidental coincidences and lacks inevitability, which is a very obvious fact.

However, the screenwriter Robert Riskin, like the director, cleverly concealed these coincidences. He paid attention to the strict structure of each section, especially in the description of the characters' personalities. He made the imaginary characters come alive from small places. Originally, they were not real, but he emphasized the exaggeration to make them almost real. From this point of view, the screenwriter was victorious.

We will not neglect Frank Capra, the author of "Lady for a Day." In "Lady for a Day," he has already given us a deep understanding. The poor old woman is pitiful all her life, but because she is deeply moving, she receives the sincere help of the governor and even the hooligans. As a result, she became a lady for a day and fulfilled her daughter's marriage to the count, and thus she herself became luxurious. This upward-climbing preaching has already given us a clear indication of his poisoning of the audience. And in this "It Happened One Night"? His theme is: As long as the unemployed newspaper reporter has firm ambition and personality, and can sincerely love a rich daughter, the result is that he can become a dragon-riding son-in-law of a big banker and become unexpectedly wealthy. This vulgar philosophy is completely consistent with that expressed in "Lady for a Day."

A clumsy preaching will not cause any bad shaking to the arrogant audience, but he uses so-called excellent expressive skills, exaggeratingly making film art a tool of deception, making people moved by his yellow preaching, which is a terrible poisoning for the relatively backward audience.

Standing on the standpoint of appreciating old film art, we acknowledge that this Frank Capra, who truly comes from the film industry, does have his own unique features. As far as this film is concerned, he displays his talents in all aspects. Lively and compact montage, harmonious tones, rich interest, flexible angles, and the grasp of the characters' personalities are all purely cinematic and very successfully achieve his success. If only from these places, we have no way to find his shortcomings. We must integrate content and form and criticize him as a whole. Then, we require film art to be 100% expressive of truth, and definitely not use it as a deceptive preaching. Otherwise, it only shows that American film art has developed to its highest point and is heading towards decline. Using highly expressive skills to serve yellow propaganda will make this propaganda deeper and more terrifying. Film art has become a cursed thing in Capra's hands. This is what we should seriously point out.

Four Stars of Tianyi Fall 251

— Ying

It is midsummer, the epidemic is rampant, and those who die from heatstroke are piled up everywhere. Although Tianyi Company has tried its best to resist the summer heat, in the past five days, four major stars have died in succession.

Yu Guang died of heatstroke and alcohol poisoning. Chen Yumei grieved over Yu Guang's death and died from one mournful cry. Ye Qiuxin was forced by the summer heat, dizzy and unconscious, and was hit in the head by a car and died in the hospital. Fan Xuepeng wanted to go to Lushan to escape the summer heat, but was crushed by a train.

Readers reading this will surely slap the table and exclaim for Tianyi Company. In fact, readers should calmly read on. The above is all in the play. Yu Guang and Chen Yumei are in "Baihua Zhou," and Ye Qiuxin and Fan Yunpeng are in "Renzhu."

Film Novel

A Good Son and a Good Wife (Borntobekissed) (6) 252

— Xin Zhi

Jidi giggled and said, "Oh, that's the little friend!" That handsome young man said apologetically, "I heard you praise me like that, and I felt a little dizzy in my head, and I didn't expect to overturn the car." Yi Di asked, "What's your name?" That young man looked at her and smiled, "Tom." Yi Di looked at him and saw that he was indeed a very handsome young man, so she couldn't help but smile and say, "Okay, Tom, we've let you hear everything we said." Tom then took the opportunity to threaten, "I'll treat you to lunch, okay? Otherwise, I'll tell Pan Shen about what you said." Jidi also pleaded from the side, "Yi Di, promise him!" Tom looked at Jidi and said, "In Li Dao, there's also a very good-looking swimming teacher." Yi Di finally agreed, partly because Jidi was begging so hard that she couldn't refuse, and partly because Tom kept smiling at her like that, making her unable to resist.

They had lunch in Li Dao and then ran to the beach to swim. There was indeed a swimming teacher there, as good-looking as Tom had said. Jidi got to know the swimming teacher and the two of them hid behind a sand dune to talk about love, leaving Tom to accompany Yi Di to rest under a large parasol. Tom kept looking at Yi Di, as if reluctant to let go. After Yi Di swam for a while, she lay on the sand panting娇喘嘘, and Tom couldn't help but feel moved. He asked, "Comfortable?" Yi Di looked at him and also felt her heart pounding, but she reminded herself that she was a good woman and that she had a specific purpose in coming to Palm Beach. She kept the name Pan Qi firmly in her mind. So she reluctantly replied, "Of course, very comfortable." Tom said, "We can come here to play every day." Yi Di suddenly sat up and said, "Tom, listen, we have a lot of things in common. We can be considered people of the same path. I don't need to pretend with you anymore…" Tom heard that and felt it was completely his father's tone, so he couldn't help but exclaim, "Oh? What's wrong?" Yi Di said, "To put it simply, my purpose in coming here is to marry a millionaire." Tom said, "Are you talking about Mr. Pan?" Yi Di said, "That's not necessarily the case. Maybe his friends are also okay." Tom also sat up and said slowly, "Money is not the most important thing. The most important thing is that you can be with someone who can make you crazy." He leaned closer to her, and in a moment, their faces were close together. Yi Di felt very anxious and wanted to stand up, but Tom tripped her with his foot and knocked her down. Tom took the opportunity of her falling down, put his arm around her, and kissed her in his arms. In that instant, Yi Di forgot her restraint and couldn't help but let him kiss her. But she suddenly pushed him away again, used all her strength to climb up, and said sternly to Tom, "Quick, give me the key to the bathroom!" Tom pleaded, "Yi Di, I won't disappoint you." Yi Di looked at him again and娇嗔 said, "Why can't we be true friends? I'm all sincerity." He laughed. She was so cute when she was angry. Alas, what would she be like when she was happy? So he said, "Okay, let's be true friends. I'll give you a true proof first… Look!" He pointed to a beautiful yacht on the sea in front and said, "That's Pan Qi's yacht." Yi Di looked over, overjoyed, and said, "Oh, it really is!" Tom said, "Look, the owner's flag is flying high, that means Pan Qi is on the boat now. Let me call a small boat to send you to the yacht, okay?" Yi Di heard that, opened her big eyes,转咕噜三噜, and said: "You are really a good person, but let me call the boat myself." She was calculating in her heart that she wanted to get rid of the young man. (To be continued)
